   1: import 'package:firebase_core/firebase_core.dart';
   2: import 'package:flutter/material.dart';
   3: import 'package:flutter_riverpod/flutter_riverpod.dart';
   4: import 'package:lavamax/core/theme/app_theme.dart';
   5: import 'package:lavamax/firebase_options.dart';
   6: import 'package:lavamax/presentation/providers/auth_provider.dart';
   7: import 'package:lavamax/presentation/screens/auth_screen.dart';
   8: import 'package:lavamax/presentation/screens/home_screen.dart';
   9: void main() async {
  10:   WidgetsFlutterBinding.ensureInitialized();
  11:   await Firebase.initializeApp(
  12:     options: DefaultFirebaseOptions.currentPlatform,
  13:   );
  14:   runApp(
  15:     const ProviderScope(
  16:       child: LavaMaxApp(),
  17:     ),
  18:   );
  19: }
  20: class LavaMaxApp extends ConsumerWidget {
  21:   const LavaMaxApp({super.key});
  22:   @override
  23:   Widget build(BuildContext context, WidgetRef ref) {
  24:     final authState = ref.watch(authStateProvider);
  25:     return MaterialApp(
  26:       title: 'LavaMax',
  27:       debugShowCheckedModeBanner: false,
  28:       theme: AppTheme.lightTheme,
  29:       home: authState.when(
  30:         data: (user) => user != null ? const HomeScreen() : const AuthScreen(),
  31:         loading: () => const Scaffold(
  32:           body: Center(child: CircularProgressIndicator()),
  33:         ),
  34:         error: (_, _) => const AuthScreen(),
  35:       ),
  36:     );
  37:   }
  38: }

ARQUIVO: C:\Users\Alex Salles\Apps - desenvolvimento\lavamax\lib\core\utils\formatters.dart
==================================================
   1: import 'package:intl/intl.dart';
   2: /// Formata um valor double para moeda BRL: R$ 1.500,00
   3: String formatBrl(double value) {
   4:   return NumberFormat.currency(
   5:     locale: 'pt_BR',
   6:     symbol: 'R\$',
   7:     decimalDigits: 2,
   8:   ).format(value);
   9: }
  10: /// Formata uma placa para o padrão XXX-XXXX.
  11: /// Remove traços existentes antes de reformatar.
  12: String formatPlate(String plate) {
  13:   final clean = plate.toUpperCase().replaceAll('-', '').replaceAll(' ', '');
  14:   if (clean.length >= 4) {
  15:     return '${clean.substring(0, 3)}-${clean.substring(3)}';
  16:   }
  17:   return plate.toUpperCase();
  18: }
  19: /// Formata um telefone para (XX)XXXXX-XXXX ou (XX)XXXX-XXXX.
  20: /// Aceita apenas dígitos; ignora formatação existente.
  21: String formatPhone(String phone) {
  22:   final digits = phone.replaceAll(RegExp(r'\D'), '');
  23:   if (digits.length == 11) {
  24:     // Celular: (XX)XXXXX-XXXX
  25:     return '(${digits.substring(0, 2)})${digits.substring(2, 7)}-${digits.substring(7)}';
  26:   }
  27:   if (digits.length == 10) {
  28:     // Fixo: (XX)XXXX-XXXX
  29:     return '(${digits.substring(0, 2)})${digits.substring(2, 6)}-${digits.substring(6)}';
  30:   }
  31:   // Retorna original se não se encaixar
  32:   return phone;
  33: }

   1: import 'package:cloud_firestore/cloud_firestore.dart';
   2: class BranchModel {
   3:   final String id;
   4:   final String name;
   5:   final String address;
   6:   final String phone;
   7:   final String city;
   8:   final String state;
   9:   final double latitude;
  10:   final double longitude;
  11:   final bool isActive;
  12:   final DateTime createdAt;
  13:   final DateTime updatedAt;
  14:   /// Se preenchido, apenas veículos dessa marca podem agendar nesta filial.
  15:   /// Valor vem do campo `allowed_brand` no Firestore (ex: "Porsche").
  16:   /// Nulo significa sem restrição de marca.
  17:   final String? allowedBrand;
  18:   BranchModel({
  19:     required this.id,
  20:     required this.name,
  21:     required this.address,
  22:     required this.phone,
  23:     required this.city,
  24:     required this.state,
  25:     required this.latitude,
  26:     required this.longitude,
  27:     required this.isActive,
  28:     required this.createdAt,
  29:     required this.updatedAt,
  30:     this.allowedBrand,
  31:   });
  32:   factory BranchModel.fromFirestore(DocumentSnapshot doc) {
  33:     final data = doc.data() as Map<String, dynamic>;
  34:     return BranchModel(
  35:       id: doc.id,
  36:       name: data['name'] ?? '',
  37:       address: data['address'] ?? '',
  38:       phone: data['phone'] ?? '',
  39:       city: data['city'] ?? '',
  40:       state: data['state'] ?? '',
  41:       latitude: (data['latitude'] ?? 0.0).toDouble(),
  42:       longitude: (data['longitude'] ?? 0.0).toDouble(),
  43:       isActive: data['is_active'] ?? true,
  44:       createdAt: (data['created_at'] as Timestamp?)?.toDate() ?? DateTime.now(),
  45:       updatedAt: (data['updated_at'] as Timestamp?)?.toDate() ?? DateTime.now(),
  46:       allowedBrand: data['allowed_brand'] as String?,
  47:     );
  48:   }
  49:   Map<String, dynamic> toFirestore() {
  50:     return {
  51:       'name': name,
  52:       'address': address,
  53:       'phone': phone,
  54:       'city': city,
  55:       'state': state,
  56:       'latitude': latitude,
  57:       'longitude': longitude,
  58:       'is_active': isActive,
  59:       'created_at': FieldValue.serverTimestamp(),
  60:       'updated_at': FieldValue.serverTimestamp(),
  61:       if (allowedBrand != null) 'allowed_brand': allowedBrand,
  62:     };
  63:   }
  64:   BranchModel copyWith({
  65:     String? id,
  66:     String? name,
  67:     String? address,
  68:     String? phone,
  69:     String? city,
  70:     String? state,
  71:     double? latitude,
  72:     double? longitude,
  73:     bool? isActive,
  74:     DateTime? createdAt,
  75:     DateTime? updatedAt,
  76:     String? allowedBrand,
  77:   }) {
  78:     return BranchModel(
  79:       id: id ?? this.id,
  80:       name: name ?? this.name,
  81:       address: address ?? this.address,
  82:       phone: phone ?? this.phone,
  83:       city: city ?? this.city,
  84:       state: state ?? this.state,
  85:       latitude: latitude ?? this.latitude,

   1: class UserModel {
   2:   final String uid;
   3:   final String name;
   4:   final String email;
   5:   final String role;
   6:   final String identifier;
   7:   final String identifierType; // 'username' | 'cpf' | 'phone'
   8:   final String phone;
   9:   final String whatsapp;
  10:   final String address;
  11:   const UserModel({
  12:     required this.uid,
  13:     required this.name,
  14:     required this.email,
  15:     required this.role,
  16:     required this.identifier,
  17:     required this.identifierType,
  18:     this.phone = '',
  19:     this.whatsapp = '',
  20:     this.address = '',
  21:   });
  22:   bool get isMaster => role == 'master';
  23:   factory UserModel.fromMap(String uid, Map<String, dynamic> map) {
  24:     return UserModel(
  25:       uid: uid,
  26:       name: map['name'] as String? ?? '',
  27:       email: map['email'] as String? ?? '',
  28:       role: map['role'] as String? ?? 'user',
  29:       identifier: map['identifier'] as String? ?? '',
  30:       identifierType: map['identifier_type'] as String? ?? 'username',
  31:       phone: map['phone'] as String? ?? '',
  32:       whatsapp: map['whatsapp'] as String? ?? '',
  33:       address: map['address'] as String? ?? '',
  34:     );
  35:   }
  36:   Map<String, dynamic> toMap() {
  37:     return {
  38:       'name': name,
  39:       'email': email,

   1: import 'package:cloud_firestore/cloud_firestore.dart';
   2: class VehicleModel {
   3:   final String id;
   4:   final String brandId;
   5:   final String brand; // resolvido em runtime via brandId — não salvo no Firestore
   6:   final String model;
   7:   final int year;
   8:   final String plate;
   9:   final DateTime createdAt;
  10:   VehicleModel({
  11:     required this.id,
  12:     required this.brandId,
  13:     this.brand = '',
  14:     required this.model,
  15:     required this.year,
  16:     required this.plate,
  17:     required this.createdAt,
  18:   });
  19:   String get displayName => '$brand $model ($year) — $plate';
  20:   factory VehicleModel.fromFirestore(DocumentSnapshot doc) {
  21:     final data = doc.data() as Map<String, dynamic>;
  22:     return VehicleModel(
  23:       id: doc.id,
  24:       brandId: data['brand_id'] ?? '',
  25:       brand: '',
  26:       model: data['model'] ?? '',
  27:       year: data['year'] ?? 0,
  28:       plate: data['plate'] ?? '',
  29:       createdAt:
  30:           (data['created_at'] as Timestamp?)?.toDate() ?? DateTime.now(),
  31:     );
  32:   }
  33:   Map<String, dynamic> toFirestore() {
  34:     return {
  35:       'brand_id': brandId,
  36:       'model': model,
  37:       'year': year,
  38:       'plate': plate.toUpperCase(),
  39:       'created_at': FieldValue.serverTimestamp(),
  40:     };
  41:   }
  42:   VehicleModel copyWith({
  43:     String? id,
  44:     String? brandId,
  45:     String? brand,
  46:     String? model,
  47:     int? year,
  48:     String? plate,
  49:     DateTime? createdAt,
  50:   }) {
  51:     return VehicleModel(
  52:       id: id ?? this.id,
  53:       brandId: brandId ?? this.brandId,
  54:       brand: brand ?? this.brand,
  55:       model: model ?? this.model,
  56:       year: year ?? this.year,
  57:       plate: plate ?? this.plate,
  58:       createdAt: createdAt ?? this.createdAt,
  59:     );
  60:   }
  61: }

   1: import 'package:cloud_firestore/cloud_firestore.dart';
   2: import 'package:lavamax/data/models/appointment_model.dart';
   3: import 'package:lavamax/data/models/credit_model.dart';
   4: class AppointmentRepository {
   5:   final FirebaseFirestore _firestore;
   6:   AppointmentRepository(this._firestore);
   7:   /// Cria o agendamento, reserva o slot e — opcionalmente — marca o crédito
   8:   /// como usado, tudo numa única transação atômica.
   9:   ///
  10:   /// [useCreditId] deve ser o ID do documento em `credits` a ser consumido.
  11:   /// Se null ou vazio, nenhum crédito é alterado.
  12:   Future<void> createAppointmentAndReserveSlot(
  13:     AppointmentModel appointment, {
  14:     String? useCreditId,
  15:   }) async {
  16:     await _firestore.runTransaction((transaction) async {
  17:       final slotRef =
  18:           _firestore.collection('slots').doc(appointment.slotId);
  19:       final slotDoc = await transaction.get(slotRef);
  20:       if (!slotDoc.exists) {
  21:         throw Exception('Horario nao encontrado.');
  22:       }
  23:       final slotData = slotDoc.data() as Map<String, dynamic>;
  24:       if (!(slotData['is_available'] as bool? ?? false)) {
  25:         throw Exception(
  26:             'Este horario acabou de ser reservado por outro cliente. '
  27:             'Por favor, escolha outro.');
  28:       }
  29:       // Consome o crédito dentro da transação (atomicamente)
  30:       if (useCreditId != null && useCreditId.isNotEmpty) {
  31:         final creditRef =
  32:             _firestore.collection('credits').doc(useCreditId);
  33:         final creditDoc = await transaction.get(creditRef);
  34:         if (creditDoc.exists &&
  35:             creditDoc.data()?['status'] ==
  36:                 'active') {
  37:           transaction.update(creditRef, {
  38:             'status': 'used',
  39:             'used_at': FieldValue.serverTimestamp(),
  40:           });
  41:         }
  42:       }
  43:       final appointmentRef =
  44:           _firestore.collection('appointments').doc(appointment.id);
  45:       transaction.set(appointmentRef, appointment.toFirestore());
  46:       transaction.update(slotRef, {
  47:         'is_available': false,
  48:         'appointment_id': appointment.id,
  49:         'updated_at': FieldValue.serverTimestamp(),
  50:       });
  51:     });
  52:   }
  53:   Future<List<AppointmentModel>> getAppointmentsByCustomer(
  54:       String customerId) async {
  55:     try {
  56:       final snapshot = await _firestore
  57:           .collection('appointments')
  58:           .where('customer_id', isEqualTo: customerId)
  59:           .get();
  60:       final list = snapshot.docs
  61:           .map((doc) => AppointmentModel.fromFirestore(doc))
  62:           .toList();
  63:       list.sort(
  64:           (a, b) => b.appointmentDate.compareTo(a.appointmentDate));
  65:       return list;
  66:     } catch (e) {
  67:       throw Exception('Erro ao buscar agendamentos: $e');
  68:     }
  69:   }
  70:   /// Busca todos os agendamentos (admin). Limitado a 200 por carga.
  71:   Future<List<AppointmentModel>> getAllAppointments({
  72:     int limit = 200,
  73:   }) async {
  74:     try {
  75:       final snapshot = await _firestore
  76:           .collection('appointments')
  77:           .orderBy('appointment_date', descending: true)
  78:           .limit(limit)
  79:           .get();
  80:       return snapshot.docs
  81:           .map((doc) => AppointmentModel.fromFirestore(doc))
  82:           .toList();
  83:     } catch (e) {
  84:       throw Exception('Erro ao buscar agendamentos: $e');
  85:     }
  86:   }
  87:   Future<AppointmentModel?> getAppointmentById(
  88:       String appointmentId) async {
  89:     try {
  90:       final doc = await _firestore
  91:           .collection('appointments')
  92:           .doc(appointmentId)
  93:           .get();
  94:       if (doc.exists) return AppointmentModel.fromFirestore(doc);
  95:       return null;
  96:     } catch (e) {
  97:       throw Exception('Erro ao buscar agendamento: $e');
  98:     }
  99:   }
 100:   Future<void> updateAppointmentStatus(
 101:       String appointmentId, String status) async {
 102:     try {
 103:       await _firestore
 104:           .collection('appointments')
 105:           .doc(appointmentId)
 106:           .update({
 107:         'status': status,
 108:         'updated_at': FieldValue.serverTimestamp(),
 109:       });
 110:     } catch (e) {
 111:       throw Exception('Erro ao atualizar agendamento: $e');
 112:     }
 113:   }
 114:   /// Cancela o agendamento, libera o slot e gera crédito para o cliente.
 115:   /// O crédito é criado após a transação (limitação do SDK: queries de
 116:   /// coleção não são permitidas dentro de transações Firestore). O erro
 117:   /// é propagado normalmente — sem catch silencioso.
 118:   Future<void> cancelAppointment(
 119:     AppointmentModel appointment,
 120:     String customerName,
 121:   ) async {
 122:     try {
 123:       await _firestore.runTransaction((transaction) async {
 124:         final appointmentRef = _firestore
 125:             .collection('appointments')
 126:             .doc(appointment.id);
 127:         final appointmentDoc =
 128:             await transaction.get(appointmentRef);
 129:         if (!appointmentDoc.exists) {
 130:           throw Exception('Agendamento nao encontrado.');
 131:         }
 132:         transaction.update(appointmentRef, {
 133:           'status': 'canceled',
 134:           'updated_at': FieldValue.serverTimestamp(),
 135:         });
 136:         final slotId = appointment.slotId;
 137:         if (slotId.isNotEmpty) {
 138:           final slotRef =
 139:               _firestore.collection('slots').doc(slotId);
 140:           transaction.update(slotRef, {
 141:             'is_available': true,
 142:             'appointment_id': null,
 143:             'updated_at': FieldValue.serverTimestamp(),
 144:           });
 145:         }
 146:       });
 147:       // Cria o crédito após a transação — erro é propagado (sem catch silencioso)
 148:       final credit = CreditModel(
 149:         id: '',
 150:         customerId: appointment.customerId,
 151:         customerName: customerName,
 152:         branchId: appointment.branchId,
 153:         branchName: appointment.branchName,
 154:         originAppointmentId: appointment.id,
 155:         serviceName: appointment.serviceName,
 156:         status: 'active',
 157:         createdAt: DateTime.now(),
 158:       );
 159:       await _firestore.collection('credits').add(credit.toFirestore());
 160:     } catch (e) {
 161:       throw Exception('Erro ao cancelar agendamento: $e');
 162:     }
 163:   }
 164:   /// Remove o documento permanentemente e libera o slot se necessário.
 165:   Future<void> deleteAppointment(String appointmentId) async {
 166:     try {
 167:       await _firestore.runTransaction((transaction) async {
 168:         final appointmentRef = _firestore
 169:             .collection('appointments')
 170:             .doc(appointmentId);
 171:         final appointmentDoc =
 172:             await transaction.get(appointmentRef);
 173:         if (!appointmentDoc.exists) {
 174:           throw Exception('Agendamento nao encontrado.');
 175:         }
 176:         final data = appointmentDoc.data()!;
 177:         final status = data['status'] as String? ?? '';
 178:         final slotId = data['slot_id'] as String?;
 179:         if (status != 'canceled' &&
 180:             slotId != null &&
 181:             slotId.isNotEmpty) {
 182:           final slotRef =
 183:               _firestore.collection('slots').doc(slotId);
 184:           transaction.update(slotRef, {
 185:             'is_available': true,
 186:             'appointment_id': null,
 187:             'updated_at': FieldValue.serverTimestamp(),
 188:           });
 189:         }
 190:         transaction.delete(appointmentRef);
 191:       });
 192:     } catch (e) {
 193:       throw Exception('Erro ao excluir agendamento: $e');
 194:     }
 195:   }
 196:   /// Cancela agendamentos ativos (liberando slots) e exclui todos os
 197:   /// agendamentos do cliente. Usado ao excluir um usuário.
 198:   /// Não gera crédito — a exclusão é uma ação administrativa.
 199:   Future<int> cancelAndDeleteAllByCustomer(String customerId) async {
 200:     try {
 201:       final snap = await _firestore
 202:           .collection('appointments')
 203:           .where('customer_id', isEqualTo: customerId)
 204:           .get();
 205:       if (snap.docs.isEmpty) return 0;
 206:       final batch = _firestore.batch();
 207:       for (final doc in snap.docs) {
 208:         final data = doc.data();
 209:         final status = data['status'] as String? ?? '';
 210:         final slotId = data['slot_id'] as String? ?? '';
 211:         if (status != 'canceled' &&
 212:             status != 'completed' &&
 213:             slotId.isNotEmpty) {
 214:           final slotRef =
 215:               _firestore.collection('slots').doc(slotId);
 216:           batch.update(slotRef, {
 217:             'is_available': true,
 218:             'appointment_id': null,
 219:             'updated_at': FieldValue.serverTimestamp(),
 220:           });
 221:         }
 222:         batch.delete(doc.reference);
 223:       }
 224:       await batch.commit();
 225:       return snap.docs.length;
 226:     } catch (e) {
 227:       throw Exception('Erro ao excluir agendamentos do usuario: $e');
 228:     }
 229:   }
 230: }

   1: import 'package:cloud_firestore/cloud_firestore.dart';
   2: import 'package:lavamax/data/models/branch_model.dart';
   3: class BranchRepository {
   4:   final FirebaseFirestore _firestore;
   5:   BranchRepository(this._firestore);
   6:   /// Stream em tempo real — qualquer alteração no Firestore
   7:   /// é refletida imediatamente no app, sem reinstalar.
   8:   Stream<List<BranchModel>> watchAllBranches() {
   9:     return _firestore
  10:         .collection('branches')
  11:         .where('is_active', isEqualTo: true)
  12:         .snapshots()
  13:         .map((snap) => snap.docs
  14:             .map((doc) => BranchModel.fromFirestore(doc))
  15:             .toList());
  16:   }
  17:   Future<List<BranchModel>> getAllBranches() async {
  18:     try {
  19:       final snapshot = await _firestore
  20:           .collection('branches')
  21:           .where('is_active', isEqualTo: true)
  22:           .get();
  23:       return snapshot.docs
  24:           .map((doc) => BranchModel.fromFirestore(doc))
  25:           .toList();
  26:     } catch (e) {
  27:       throw Exception('Erro ao buscar filiais: $e');
  28:     }
  29:   }
  30:   Future<BranchModel?> getBranchById(String branchId) async {
  31:     try {
  32:       final doc =
  33:           await _firestore.collection('branches').doc(branchId).get();
  34:       if (doc.exists) {
  35:         return BranchModel.fromFirestore(doc);
  36:       }
  37:       return null;
  38:     } catch (e) {
  39:       throw Exception('Erro ao buscar filial: $e');
  40:     }
  41:   }
  42:   Future<void> createBranch(BranchModel branch) async {
  43:     try {
  44:       await _firestore
  45:           .collection('branches')
  46:           .doc(branch.id)
  47:           .set(branch.toFirestore());
  48:     } catch (e) {
  49:       throw Exception('Erro ao criar filial: $e');
  50:     }
  51:   }
  52:   Future<void> updateBranch(BranchModel branch) async {
  53:     try {
  54:       await _firestore
  55:           .collection('branches')
  56:           .doc(branch.id)
  57:           .update(branch.toFirestore());
  58:     } catch (e) {
  59:       throw Exception('Erro ao atualizar filial: $e');
  60:     }
  61:   }

   1: import 'package:cloud_firestore/cloud_firestore.dart';
   2: import '../models/consultant_model.dart';
   3: class ConsultantRepository {
   4:   final FirebaseFirestore _db;
   5:   ConsultantRepository(this._db);
   6:   Stream<List<ConsultantModel>> watchByBranch(String branchId) {
   7:     return _db
   8:         .collection('consultants')
   9:         .where('branch_id', isEqualTo: branchId)
  10:         .where('is_active', isEqualTo: true)
  11:         .snapshots()
  12:         .map((s) {
  13:       final list = s.docs.map(ConsultantModel.fromFirestore).toList();
  14:       list.sort((a, b) => a.name.compareTo(b.name));
  15:       return list;
  16:     });
  17:   }
  18:   Future<List<ConsultantModel>> getByBranch(String branchId) async {
  19:     final snap = await _db
  20:         .collection('consultants')
  21:         .where('branch_id', isEqualTo: branchId)
  22:         .where('is_active', isEqualTo: true)
  23:         .get();
  24:     final list = snap.docs.map(ConsultantModel.fromFirestore).toList();
  25:     list.sort((a, b) => a.name.compareTo(b.name));
  26:     return list;
  27:   }
  28:   /// Verifica se o consultor já tem agendamento no mesmo slot (mesmo horário).
  29:   Future<bool> hasConflictAtSlot(
  30:       String consultantId, DateTime slotTime) async {
  31:     final snap = await _db
  32:         .collection('appointments')
  33:         .where('consultant_id', isEqualTo: consultantId)
  34:         .where('appointment_date',
  35:             isEqualTo: Timestamp.fromDate(slotTime))
  36:         .get();
  37:     return snap.docs.isNotEmpty;
  38:   }
  39:   /// Retorna o consultor mais disponível no dia usando UMA única query de
  40:   /// agendamentos por filial — elimina o padrão N+1 da versão anterior.
  41:   ///
  42:   /// Índice composto necessário no Firestore:
  43:   ///   Coleção: appointments | Campos: branch_id ASC · appointment_date ASC
  44:   Future<ConsultantModel?> getMostAvailable(
  45:       String branchId, DateTime day) async {
  46:     final consultants = await getByBranch(branchId);
  47:     if (consultants.isEmpty) return null;
  48:     final start = DateTime(day.year, day.month, day.day);
  49:     final end = start.add(const Duration(days: 1));
  50:     // Uma única query para todos os agendamentos do dia nesta filial
  51:     final snap = await _db
  52:         .collection('appointments')
  53:         .where('branch_id', isEqualTo: branchId)
  54:         .where('appointment_date',
  55:             isGreaterThanOrEqualTo: Timestamp.fromDate(start))
  56:         .where('appointment_date',
  57:             isLessThan: Timestamp.fromDate(end))
  58:         .get();
  59:     // Conta agendamentos por consultor em Dart (zero queries extras)
  60:     final counts = <String, int>{
  61:       for (final c in consultants) c.id: 0,
  62:     };
  63:     for (final doc in snap.docs) {
  64:       final cId = doc.data()['consultant_id'] as String?;
  65:       if (cId != null && counts.containsKey(cId)) {
  66:         counts[cId] = counts[cId]! + 1;
  67:       }
  68:     }
  69:     ConsultantModel? best;
  70:     int bestCount = 999;
  71:     for (final c in consultants) {
  72:       final count = counts[c.id] ?? 0;
  73:       if (count < bestCount) {
  74:         bestCount = count;
  75:         best = c;
  76:       }
  77:     }
  78:     return best;
  79:   }
  80:   Future<void> create(ConsultantModel consultant) async {
  81:     await _db.collection('consultants').add(consultant.toFirestore());
  82:   }
  83:   Future<void> update(String id, Map<String, dynamic> data) async {
  84:     await _db.collection('consultants').doc(id).update(data);
  85:   }
  86:   Future<void> delete(String id) async {
  87:     await _db.collection('consultants').doc(id).delete();
  88:   }
  89: }

   1: import 'package:cloud_firestore/cloud_firestore.dart';
   2: import 'package:lavamax/data/models/credit_model.dart';
   3: class CreditRepository {
   4:   final FirebaseFirestore _db;
   5:   CreditRepository(this._db);
   6:   static const int _defaultMaxCredits = 2;
   7:   /// Retorna o limite máximo de créditos ativos por cliente,
   8:   /// conforme configurado pelo admin em config/credits.
   9:   Future<int> getMaxCredits() async {
  10:     try {
  11:       final doc =
  12:           await _db.collection('config').doc('credits').get();
  13:       if (doc.exists) {
  14:         return (doc.data()?['max_credits_per_customer'] as int?) ??
  15:             _defaultMaxCredits;
  16:       }
  17:     } catch (_) {}
  18:     return _defaultMaxCredits;
  19:   }
  20:   Future<void> setMaxCredits(int value) async {
  21:     await _db
  22:         .collection('config')
  23:         .doc('credits')
  24:         .set({'max_credits_per_customer': value}, SetOptions(merge: true));
  25:   }
  26:   /// Verifica se o cliente já atingiu o limite de créditos ativos.
  27:   /// Usado para bloquear o cancelamento antes de executá-lo.
  28:   Future<bool> hasReachedLimit(String customerId) async {
  29:     final maxCredits = await getMaxCredits();
  30:     final activeSnap = await _db
  31:         .collection('credits')
  32:         .where('customer_id', isEqualTo: customerId)
  33:         .where('status', isEqualTo: 'active')
  34:         .get();
  35:     return activeSnap.docs.length >= maxCredits;
  36:   }
  37:   /// Retorna créditos ativos do cliente numa filial específica.
  38:   Future<List<CreditModel>> getActiveCredits(
  39:       String customerId, String branchId) async {
  40:     final snap = await _db
  41:         .collection('credits')
  42:         .where('customer_id', isEqualTo: customerId)
  43:         .where('branch_id', isEqualTo: branchId)
  44:         .where('status', isEqualTo: 'active')
  45:         .get();
  46:     return snap.docs.map(CreditModel.fromFirestore).toList();
  47:   }
  48:   /// Retorna todos os créditos do cliente (qualquer status).
  49:   Future<List<CreditModel>> getCreditsForCustomer(
  50:       String customerId) async {
  51:     final snap = await _db
  52:         .collection('credits')
  53:         .where('customer_id', isEqualTo: customerId)
  54:         .get();
  55:     final list = snap.docs.map(CreditModel.fromFirestore).toList();
  56:     list.sort((a, b) => b.createdAt.compareTo(a.createdAt));
  57:     return list;
  58:   }
  59:   /// Retorna todos os créditos (admin).
  60:   Future<List<CreditModel>> getAllCredits() async {
  61:     final snap = await _db.collection('credits').get();
  62:     final list = snap.docs.map(CreditModel.fromFirestore).toList();
  63:     list.sort((a, b) => b.createdAt.compareTo(a.createdAt));
  64:     return list;
  65:   }
  66:   /// Cria um crédito. Verifica o limite antes de criar.
  67:   /// Lança exceção se o limite já foi atingido.
  68:   Future<void> createCredit(CreditModel credit) async {
  69:     final maxCredits = await getMaxCredits();
  70:     final activeSnap = await _db
  71:         .collection('credits')
  72:         .where('customer_id', isEqualTo: credit.customerId)
  73:         .where('status', isEqualTo: 'active')
  74:         .get();
  75:     if (activeSnap.docs.length >= maxCredits) {
  76:       throw Exception(
  77:           'Limite de creditos atingido para este cliente.');
  78:     }
  79:     await _db.collection('credits').add(credit.toFirestore());
  80:   }
  81:   /// Marca o primeiro crédito ativo do cliente na filial como 'used'.
  82:   /// Retorna o id do crédito usado, ou null se não havia crédito.
  83:   Future<String?> useCredit(
  84:       String customerId, String branchId) async {
  85:     final actives = await getActiveCredits(customerId, branchId);
  86:     if (actives.isEmpty) return null;
  87:     final credit = actives.first;
  88:     await _db.collection('credits').doc(credit.id).update({
  89:       'status': 'used',
  90:       'used_at': FieldValue.serverTimestamp(),
  91:     });
  92:     return credit.id;
  93:   }
  94:   /// Cancela um crédito manualmente (admin).
  95:   Future<void> cancelCredit(String creditId) async {
  96:     await _db.collection('credits').doc(creditId).update({
  97:       'status': 'canceled',
  98:     });
  99:   }
 100:   /// Reativa um crédito cancelado (admin).
 101:   Future<void> reactivateCredit(String creditId) async {
 102:     await _db.collection('credits').doc(creditId).update({
 103:       'status': 'active',
 104:       'used_at': null,
 105:     });
 106:   }
 107: }

   1: import 'package:cloud_firestore/cloud_firestore.dart';
   2: import 'package:lavamax/data/models/service_model.dart';
   3: class ServiceRepository {
   4:   final FirebaseFirestore _firestore;
   5:   ServiceRepository(this._firestore);
   6:   Future<List<ServiceModel>> getAllServices() async {
   7:     try {
   8:       final snapshot = await _firestore
   9:           .collection('services')
  10:           .where('is_active', isEqualTo: true)
  11:           .get();
  12:       return snapshot.docs
  13:           .map((doc) => ServiceModel.fromFirestore(doc))
  14:           .toList();
  15:     } catch (e) {
  16:       throw Exception('Erro ao buscar serviços: $e');
  17:     }
  18:   }
  19:   Future<ServiceModel?> getServiceById(String serviceId) async {
  20:     try {
  21:       final doc = await _firestore.collection('services').doc(serviceId).get();
  22:       if (doc.exists) {
  23:         return ServiceModel.fromFirestore(doc);
  24:       }
  25:       return null;
  26:     } catch (e) {
  27:       throw Exception('Erro ao buscar serviço: $e');
  28:     }
  29:   }
  30:   Future<void> createService(ServiceModel service) async {
  31:     try {
  32:       await _firestore.collection('services').doc(service.id).set(service.toFirestore());
  33:     } catch (e) {
  34:       throw Exception('Erro ao criar serviço: $e');
  35:     }
  36:   }
  37: }

   1: import 'package:cloud_firestore/cloud_firestore.dart';
   2: import 'package:lavamax/data/models/slot_model.dart';
   3: class SlotRepository {
   4:   final FirebaseFirestore _firestore;
   5:   SlotRepository(this._firestore);
   6:   Future<List<SlotModel>> getAvailableSlotsByBranch(
   7:     String branchId,
   8:     DateTime date,
   9:   ) async {
  10:     try {
  11:       final startOfDay = DateTime(date.year, date.month, date.day);
  12:       final endOfDay = startOfDay.add(const Duration(days: 1));
  13:       final snapshot = await _firestore
  14:           .collection('slots')
  15:           .where('branch_id', isEqualTo: branchId)
  16:           .where('is_available', isEqualTo: true)
  17:           .where('start_time', isGreaterThanOrEqualTo: startOfDay)
  18:           .where('start_time', isLessThan: endOfDay)
  19:           .orderBy('start_time')
  20:           .get();
  21:       return snapshot.docs
  22:           .map((doc) => SlotModel.fromFirestore(doc))
  23:           .toList();
  24:     } catch (e) {
  25:       throw Exception('Erro ao buscar horários disponíveis: $e');
  26:     }
  27:   }
  28:   /// Não usar diretamente. A reserva atômica é feita via
  29:   /// [AppointmentRepository.createAppointmentAndReserveSlot].
  30:   @Deprecated('Use AppointmentRepository.createAppointmentAndReserveSlot')
  31:   Future<void> reserveSlot(String slotId, String appointmentId) async {
  32:     try {
  33:       await _firestore.collection('slots').doc(slotId).update({
  34:         'is_available': false,
  35:         'appointment_id': appointmentId,
  36:         'updated_at': FieldValue.serverTimestamp(),
  37:       });
  38:     } catch (e) {
  39:       throw Exception('Erro ao reservar horário: $e');
  40:     }
  41:   }
  42:   /// Não usar diretamente. A liberação atômica é feita via
  43:   /// [AppointmentRepository.cancelAppointment].
  44:   @Deprecated('Use AppointmentRepository.cancelAppointment')
  45:   Future<void> releaseSlot(String slotId) async {
  46:     try {
  47:       await _firestore.collection('slots').doc(slotId).update({
  48:         'is_available': true,
  49:         'appointment_id': null,
  50:         'updated_at': FieldValue.serverTimestamp(),
  51:       });
  52:     } catch (e) {
  53:       throw Exception('Erro ao liberar horário: $e');
  54:     }
  55:   }
  56: }

ARQUIVO: C:\Users\Alex Salles\Apps - desenvolvimento\lavamax\lib\data\repositories\user_repository.dart
==================================================
   1: import 'package:cloud_firestore/cloud_firestore.dart';
   2: import '../models/user_model.dart';
   3: class UserRepository {
   4:   final FirebaseFirestore _db;
   5:   UserRepository(this._db);
   6:   Future<void> createUser(UserModel user) async {
   7:     await _db.collection('users').doc(user.uid).set(user.toMap());
   8:   }
   9:   Future<UserModel?> getUser(String uid) async {
  10:     final doc = await _db.collection('users').doc(uid).get();
  11:     if (!doc.exists || doc.data() == null) return null;
  12:     return UserModel.fromMap(uid, doc.data()!);
  13:   }
  14:   Stream<UserModel?> watchUser(String uid) {
  15:     return _db.collection('users').doc(uid).snapshots().map((snap) {
  16:       if (!snap.exists || snap.data() == null) return null;
  17:       return UserModel.fromMap(uid, snap.data()!);
  18:     });
  19:   }
  20:   Future<List<UserModel>> getAllUsers() async {
  21:     final snap = await _db.collection('users').get();
  22:     final list = snap.docs
  23:         .map((d) => UserModel.fromMap(d.id, d.data()))
  24:         .toList();
  25:     list.sort((a, b) => a.name.compareTo(b.name));
  26:     return list;
  27:   }
  28:   Future<void> updateRole(String uid, String role) async {
  29:     await _db.collection('users').doc(uid).update({'role': role});
  30:   }
  31:   /// Atualiza apenas o nome do usuário no Firestore.
  32:   /// O email de autenticação (Firebase Auth) só pode ser alterado pelo próprio
  33:   /// usuário — o admin não tem acesso via client SDK.
  34:   Future<void> updateName(String uid, {required String name}) async {
  35:     await _db.collection('users').doc(uid).update({'name': name});
  36:   }
  37:   /// Exclui apenas o documento do Firestore.
  38:   /// A conta Firebase Auth não pode ser removida pelo admin via client SDK —
  39:   /// ela permanece inativa até o próximo login do usuário.
  40:   Future<void> deleteUserData(String uid) async {
  41:     await _db.collection('users').doc(uid).delete();
  42:   }
  43: }

ARQUIVO: C:\Users\Alex Salles\Apps - desenvolvimento\lavamax\lib\data\repositories\vehicle_repository.dart
==================================================
   1: import 'package:cloud_firestore/cloud_firestore.dart';
   2: import 'package:lavamax/data/models/vehicle_brand_model.dart';
   3: import 'package:lavamax/data/models/vehicle_model.dart';
   4: class VehicleRepository {
   5:   final FirebaseFirestore _firestore;
   6:   VehicleRepository(this._firestore);
   7:   Future<List<VehicleBrandModel>> getActiveBrands() async {
   8:     try {
   9:       final snapshot = await _firestore
  10:           .collection('vehicle_brands')
  11:           .orderBy('name')
  12:           .get();
  13:       return snapshot.docs
  14:           .map((doc) => VehicleBrandModel.fromFirestore(doc))
  15:           .toList();
  16:     } catch (e) {
  17:       throw Exception('Erro ao buscar marcas');
  18:     }
  19:   }
  20:   CollectionReference _vehiclesRef(String userId) =>
  21:       _firestore.collection('users').doc(userId).collection('vehicles');
  22:   Future<List<VehicleModel>> getVehiclesByUser(String userId) async {
  23:     try {
  24:       final snapshot = await _vehiclesRef(userId)
  25:           .orderBy('created_at', descending: false)
  26:           .get();
  27:       return snapshot.docs
  28:           .map((doc) => VehicleModel.fromFirestore(doc))
  29:           .toList();
  30:     } catch (e) {
  31:       throw Exception('Erro ao buscar veiculos');
  32:     }
  33:   }
  34:   Future<VehicleModel> addVehicle(String userId, VehicleModel vehicle) async {
  35:     try {
  36:       final ref = _vehiclesRef(userId).doc();
  37:       await ref.set(vehicle.toFirestore());
  38:       final doc = await ref.get();
  39:       return VehicleModel.fromFirestore(doc);
  40:     } catch (e) {
  41:       throw Exception('Erro ao adicionar veiculo');
  42:     }
  43:   }
  44:   Future<void> deleteVehicle(String userId, String vehicleId) async {
  45:     try {
  46:       await _vehiclesRef(userId).doc(vehicleId).delete();
  47:     } catch (e) {
  48:       throw Exception('Erro ao remover veiculo');
  49:     }
  50:   }
  51: }

   1: import 'package:cloud_firestore/cloud_firestore.dart';
   2: import 'package:firebase_core/firebase_core.dart';
   3: import 'package:lavamax/firebase_options.dart';
   4: class FirebaseService {
   5:   static final FirebaseService _instance = FirebaseService._internal();
   6:   factory FirebaseService() {
   7:     return _instance;
   8:   }
   9:   FirebaseService._internal();
  10:   static Future<void> initialize() async {
  11:     await Firebase.initializeApp(
  12:       options: DefaultFirebaseOptions.currentPlatform,
  13:     );
  14:     // Enable offline persistence
  15:     FirebaseFirestore.instance.settings = const Settings(
  16:       persistenceEnabled: true, // Para o usuário poder acessar "Meus agendamentos" sem internet
  17:     );
  18:   }
  19:   FirebaseFirestore get firestore => FirebaseFirestore.instance;
  20: }

  19:       email: email.trim(),
  20:       password: password,
  21:     );
  22:     await credential.user?.updateDisplayName(name.trim());

  26:   }

ARQUIVO: C:\Users\Alex Salles\Apps - desenvolvimento\lavamax\lib\presentation\providers\connectivity_provider.dart
==================================================
   1: import 'package:connectivity_plus/connectivity_plus.dart';
   2: import 'package:flutter_riverpod/flutter_riverpod.dart';
   3: /// Emite `true` quando há conexão de rede ativa, `false` caso contrário.
   4: /// Verifica o estado inicial imediatamente ao ser criado.
   5: final connectivityProvider = StreamProvider<bool>((ref) async* {
   6:   final connectivity = Connectivity();
   7:   // Estado inicial — sem esperar o primeiro evento do stream
   8:   final initial = await connectivity.checkConnectivity();
   9:   yield initial.any((r) => r != ConnectivityResult.none);
  10:   // Atualizações em tempo real
  11:   await for (final results in connectivity.onConnectivityChanged) {
  12:     yield results.any((r) => r != ConnectivityResult.none);
  13:   }
  14: });
  15: /// Atalho síncrono: `true` = online, `false` = offline.
  16: /// Assume online durante o carregamento inicial para não bloquear desnecessariamente.
  17: final isOnlineProvider = Provider<bool>((ref) {
  18:   return ref.watch(connectivityProvider).when(
  19:     data: (online) => online,
  20:     loading: () => true,
  21:     error: (_, _) => true,
  22:   );
  23: });

   3: import 'package:lavamax/data/models/vehicle_brand_model.dart';

  12:   return repo.getActiveBrands();
  13: });
  14: final userVehiclesProvider = FutureProvider<List<VehicleModel>>((ref) async {
  15:   final uid = FirebaseAuth.instance.currentUser?.uid;
  16:   if (uid == null) return [];
  17:   final repo = ref.watch(vehicleRepositoryProvider);
  18:   final vehicles = await repo.getVehiclesByUser(uid);
  19:   final brands = await repo.getActiveBrands();
  20:   final brandMap = {for (final b in brands) b.id: b.name};
  21:   return vehicles
  22:       .map((v) => v.copyWith(brand: brandMap[v.brandId] ?? ''))
  23:       .toList();

  13: class AddVehicleScreen extends ConsumerStatefulWidget {
  14:   const AddVehicleScreen({super.key});
  15:   @override
  16:   ConsumerState<AddVehicleScreen> createState() => _AddVehicleScreenState();
  17: }
  18: class _AddVehicleScreenState extends ConsumerState<AddVehicleScreen> {
  19:   final _formKey = GlobalKey<FormState>();
  20:   final _plateController = TextEditingController();
  21:   final _yearController = TextEditingController();
  22:   VehicleBrandModel? _selectedBrand;

  25:   @override

  27:     _plateController.dispose();
  28:     _yearController.dispose();
  29:     super.dispose();

  31:   @override

  34:     return Scaffold(
  35:       appBar: CustomAppBar(title: 'Adicionar Veículo', showBackButton: true),
  36:       body: brandsAsync.when(
  37:         data: (brands) => _buildForm(brands),
  38:         loading: () => const Center(child: CircularProgressIndicator()),
  39:         error: (e, stack) =>
  40:             Center(child: Text('Erro ao carregar marcas: $e')),
  41:       ),
  42:     );
  43:   }
  44:   Widget _buildForm(List<VehicleBrandModel> brands) {
  45:     return SingleChildScrollView(
  46:       padding: const EdgeInsets.all(AppDimensions.screenPaddingHorizontal),
  47:       child: Form(
  48:         key: _formKey,
  49:         child: Column(
  50:           crossAxisAlignment: CrossAxisAlignment.stretch,
  51:           children: [
  52:             const SizedBox(height: AppDimensions.paddingMedium),
  53:             // Campo de marca — abre tela com lista completa + índice alfabético
  54:             FormField<VehicleBrandModel>(
  55:               initialValue: _selectedBrand,
  56:               validator: (v) => v == null ? 'Selecione a marca' : null,
  57:               builder: (field) => Column(
  58:                 crossAxisAlignment: CrossAxisAlignment.start,
  59:                 children: [
  60:                   InkWell(
  61:                     borderRadius: BorderRadius.circular(8),
  62:                     onTap: () async {
  63:                       final chosen =
  64:                           await Navigator.of(context).push<VehicleBrandModel>(
  65:                         MaterialPageRoute(
  66:                           builder: (_) =>
  67:                               BrandSelectionScreen(brands: brands),
  68:                         ),
  69:                       );
  70:                       if (chosen != null) {
  71:                         field.didChange(chosen);
  72:                         setState(() {
  73:                           _selectedBrand = chosen;
  74:                           _selectedModel = null;
  75:                         });
  76:                       }
  77:                     },
  78:                     child: InputDecorator(
  79:                       decoration: InputDecoration(
  80:                         labelText: 'Marca',
  81:                         prefixIcon:
  82:                             const Icon(Icons.directions_car_outlined),
  83:                         suffixIcon:
  84:                             const Icon(Icons.chevron_right_outlined),
  85:                         errorText: field.errorText,
  86:                       ),
  87:                       child: Text(
  88:                         _selectedBrand?.name ?? 'Toque para selecionar',
  89:                         style: TextStyle(
  90:                           color: _selectedBrand != null
  91:                               ? null
  92:                               : Theme.of(context).hintColor,
  93:                         ),
  94:                       ),
  95:                     ),
  96:                   ),
  97:                 ],
  98:               ),
  99:             ),
 100:             const SizedBox(height: AppDimensions.paddingMedium),
 101:             DropdownButtonFormField<String>(
 102:               decoration: const InputDecoration(
 103:                 labelText: 'Modelo',
 104:                 prefixIcon: Icon(Icons.car_repair),
 105:               ),
 106:               initialValue: _selectedModel,
 107:               items: (_selectedBrand?.models ?? [])
 108:                   .map((m) => DropdownMenuItem(value: m, child: Text(m)))
 109:                   .toList(),
 110:               onChanged: _selectedBrand == null
 111:                   ? null
 112:                   : (value) => setState(() => _selectedModel = value),
 113:               validator: (v) => v == null ? 'Selecione o modelo' : null,
 114:             ),
 115:             const SizedBox(height: AppDimensions.paddingMedium),
 116:             TextFormField(
 117:               controller: _yearController,
 118:               decoration: const InputDecoration(
 119:                 labelText: 'Ano',
 120:                 prefixIcon: Icon(Icons.calendar_today_outlined),
 121:               ),
 122:               keyboardType: TextInputType.number,
 123:               inputFormatters: [
 124:                 FilteringTextInputFormatter.digitsOnly,
 125:                 LengthLimitingTextInputFormatter(4),
 126:               ],
 127:               validator: (v) {
 128:                 final year = int.tryParse(v ?? '');
 129:                 if (year == null) return 'Digite o ano';
 130:                 if (year < 1950 || year > DateTime.now().year + 1) {
 131:                   return 'Ano inválido';
 132:                 }
 133:                 return null;
 134:               },
 135:             ),
 136:             const SizedBox(height: AppDimensions.paddingMedium),
 137:             TextFormField(
 138:               controller: _plateController,
 139:               decoration: const InputDecoration(
 140:                 labelText: 'Placa',
 141:                 prefixIcon: Icon(Icons.pin_outlined),
 142:                 hintText: 'Ex: ABC1234 ou ABC1D23',
 143:               ),
 144:               textCapitalization: TextCapitalization.characters,
 145:               inputFormatters: [
 146:                 _PlateFormatter(),
 147:               ],
 148:               validator: (v) {
 149:                 final clean = (v ?? '').replaceAll('-', '');
 150:                 if (clean.length < 7) return 'Placa inválida';
 151:                 return null;
 152:               },
 153:             ),
 154:             const SizedBox(height: AppDimensions.paddingXLarge),
 155:             ElevatedButton(
 156:               onPressed: _isLoading ? null : _save,
 157:               style: ElevatedButton.styleFrom(
 158:                 minimumSize:
 159:                     const Size.fromHeight(AppDimensions.buttonHeight),
 160:               ),
 161:               child: _isLoading
 162:                   ? const SizedBox(
 163:                       height: 20,
 164:                       width: 20,
 165:                       child: CircularProgressIndicator(
 166:                         strokeWidth: 2,
 167:                         valueColor:
 168:                             AlwaysStoppedAnimation<Color>(AppColors.white),
 169:                       ),
 170:                     )
 171:                   : const Text('Salvar Veículo'),
 172:             ),
 173:           ],
 174:         ),
 175:       ),
 176:     );
 177:   }
 178:   Future<void> _save() async {
 179:     if (!_formKey.currentState!.validate()) return;
 180:     final uid = FirebaseAuth.instance.currentUser?.uid;
 181:     if (uid == null) return;
 182:     setState(() => _isLoading = true);
 183:     try {
 184:       final vehicle = VehicleModel(
 185:         id: const Uuid().v4(),
 186:         brandId: _selectedBrand!.id,
 187:         brand: _selectedBrand!.name,
 188:         model: _selectedModel!,
 189:         year: int.parse(_yearController.text),
 190:         plate: _plateController.text.replaceAll('-', '').toUpperCase(),
 191:         createdAt: DateTime.now(),
 192:       );
 193:       await ref.read(vehicleRepositoryProvider).addVehicle(uid, vehicle);
 194:       ref.invalidate(userVehiclesProvider);
 195:       if (mounted) {
 196:         ScaffoldMessenger.of(context).showSnackBar(
 197:           const SnackBar(content: Text('Veículo adicionado com sucesso!')),
 198:         );
 199:         Navigator.of(context).pop();
 200:       }
 201:     } catch (e) {
 202:       if (mounted) {
 203:         ScaffoldMessenger.of(context)
 204:             .showSnackBar(SnackBar(content: Text('Erro ao salvar: $e')));
 205:       }
 206:     } finally {
 207:       if (mounted) setState(() => _isLoading = false);
 208:     }
 209:   }
 210: }
 211: // ── Formatter de placa: ABC-1234 ou ABC-1D23 ───────────────────
 212: class _PlateFormatter extends TextInputFormatter {
 213:   @override
 214:   TextEditingValue formatEditUpdate(
 215:       TextEditingValue oldValue, TextEditingValue newValue) {
 216:     final raw = newValue.text
 217:         .replaceAll(RegExp(r'[^A-Za-z0-9]'), '')
 218:         .toUpperCase();
 219:     final limited = raw.length > 7 ? raw.substring(0, 7) : raw;
 220:     final formatted = limited.length > 3
 221:         ? '${limited.substring(0, 3)}-${limited.substring(3)}'
 222:         : limited;
 223:     return newValue.copyWith(
 224:       text: formatted,
 225:       selection: TextSelection.collapsed(offset: formatted.length),
 226:     );
 227:   }
 228: }

  39:   Future<void> _loadConsultantAndCredit() async {
  40:     try {
  41:       final branch = ref.read(selectedBranchProvider);
  42:       final slot = ref.read(selectedSlotProvider);
  43:       if (branch == null || slot == null) return;
  44:       final uid = FirebaseAuth.instance.currentUser?.uid;
  45:       // Carrega consultor e crédito em paralelo via providers
  46:       final consultantRepo = ref.read(consultantRepositoryProvider);
  47:       final creditRepo = ref.read(creditRepositoryProvider);
  48:       final futures = await Future.wait([
  49:         consultantRepo.getMostAvailable(branch.id, slot.startTime),
  50:         if (uid != null)
  51:           creditRepo.getActiveCredits(uid, branch.id)
  52:         else
  53:           Future.value(<CreditModel>[]),
  54:       ]);
  55:       if (!mounted) return;
  56:       final best = futures[0] as dynamic;
  57:       final credits = futures[1] as List<CreditModel>;
  58:       ref.read(selectedConsultantProvider.notifier).state = best;
  59:       if (best != null) {
  60:         final conflict = await consultantRepo.hasConflictAtSlot(
  61:           best.id,
  62:           slot.startTime,
  63:         );
  64:         if (mounted) {
  65:           ref.read(consultantHasConflictProvider.notifier).state = conflict;
  66:         }
  67:       }
  68:       if (mounted) {
  69:         setState(() {
  70:           _availableCredit = credits.isNotEmpty ? credits.first : null;
  71:         });
  72:       }
  73:     } finally {
  74:       if (mounted) setState(() => _consultantsLoading = false);
  75:     }

  92:         .hasConflictAtSlot(selected.id, slot.startTime);
  93:     if (mounted) {
  94:       ref.read(consultantHasConflictProvider.notifier).state = conflict;
  95:     }

 354:   Widget _row(BuildContext context, String label, String value) {

 356:       padding: const EdgeInsets.symmetric(
 357:         vertical: AppDimensions.paddingSmall / 2,
 358:       ),

 360:         mainAxisAlignment: MainAxisAlignment.spaceBetween,

 364:             style: Theme.of(
 365:               context,
 366:             ).textTheme.bodyMedium?.copyWith(color: AppColors.grey600),
 367:           ),
 368:           Text(
 369:             value,
 370:             style: Theme.of(
 371:               context,
 372:             ).textTheme.bodyMedium?.copyWith(fontWeight: FontWeight.bold),
 373:           ),
 374:         ],
 375:       ),
 376:     );
 377:   }
 378:   Future<void> _confirm() async {
 379:     setState(() => _isLoading = true);
 380:     try {
 381:       final selectedBranch = ref.read(selectedBranchProvider);
 382:       final selectedService = ref.read(selectedServiceProvider);
 383:       final selectedSlot = ref.read(selectedSlotProvider);
 384:       final selectedVehicle = ref.read(selectedVehicleProvider);
 385:       final selectedConsultant = ref.read(selectedConsultantProvider);
 386:       final hasConflict = ref.read(consultantHasConflictProvider);
 387:       if (selectedBranch == null ||
 388:           selectedService == null ||
 389:           selectedSlot == null ||
 390:           selectedVehicle == null) {
 391:         throw Exception('Dados incompletos');
 392:       }
 393:       final currentUser = FirebaseAuth.instance.currentUser;
 394:       if (currentUser == null) {
 395:         throw Exception('Usuario nao autenticado');
 396:       }
 397:       final appointment = AppointmentModel(
 398:         id: const Uuid().v4(),
 399:         customerId: currentUser.uid,
 400:         branchId: selectedBranch.id,
 401:         branchName: selectedBranch.name,
 402:         serviceId: selectedService.id,
 403:         serviceName: selectedService.name,
 404:         slotId: selectedSlot.id,
 405:         vehicleId: selectedVehicle.id,
 406:         consultantId: selectedConsultant?.id ?? '',
 407:         consultantName: selectedConsultant?.name ?? '',
 408:         consultantPhone: selectedConsultant?.phone ?? '',
 409:         consultantConflict: hasConflict,
 410:         appointmentDate: selectedSlot.startTime,
 411:         status: 'pending',
 412:         createdAt: DateTime.now(),
 413:         updatedAt: DateTime.now(),
 414:       );
 415:       // Cria agendamento e — se houver crédito — consome-o atomicamente
 416:       await ref
 417:           .read(appointmentRepositoryProvider)
 418:           .createAppointmentAndReserveSlot(
 419:             appointment,
 420:             useCreditId: _availableCredit?.id,
 421:           );
 422:       if (mounted) {
 423:         Navigator.of(context).pushAndRemoveUntil(
 424:           MaterialPageRoute(
 425:             builder: (context) => BookingReceiptScreen(
 426:               appointment: appointment,
 427:               branch: selectedBranch,
 428:               service: selectedService,
 429:               vehicle: selectedVehicle,
 430:               usedCredit: _availableCredit != null,
 431:             ),
 432:           ),
 433:           (route) => route.isFirst,
 434:         );
 435:       }
 436:     } catch (e) {
 437:       if (mounted) {
 438:         ScaffoldMessenger.of(
 439:           context,
 440:         ).showSnackBar(SnackBar(content: Text('$e')));
 441:       }
 442:     } finally {
 443:       if (mounted) setState(() => _isLoading = false);
 444:     }
 445:   }
 446: }

  30:   });
  31:   bool get _canCancel =>
  32:       appointment.status == 'pending' ||
  33:       appointment.status == 'confirmed';
  34:   @override
  35:   Widget build(BuildContext context, WidgetRef ref) {
  36:     final dateFormat = DateFormat('dd/MM/yyyy');
  37:     final timeFormat = DateFormat('HH:mm');
  38:     final statusInfo = _statusInfo(appointment.status);
  39:     final code = appointment.id.substring(0, 8).toUpperCase();
  40:     // Resolve serviço e veículo diretamente na tela — sem depender do pai
  41:     final servicesAsync = ref.watch(servicesProvider);
  42:     final vehiclesAsync = ref.watch(userVehiclesProvider);
  43:     // Preço: busca na lista de serviços pelo serviceId
  44:     final servicePrice = servicesAsync.whenOrNull(
  45:       data: (list) {
  46:         try {
  47:           return list.firstWhere((s) => s.id == appointment.serviceId).price;
  48:         } catch (_) {
  49:           return null;
  50:         }
  51:       },
  52:     );
  53:     // Placa: busca na lista de veículos pelo vehicleId
  54:     final vehiclePlate = vehiclesAsync.whenOrNull(
  55:       data: (list) {
  56:         try {
  57:           return list.firstWhere((v) => v.id == appointment.vehicleId).plate;
  58:         } catch (_) {
  59:           return null;
  60:         }
  61:       },
  62:     );
  63:     // Verifica se o usuário atual é o dono — para mostrar veículos
  64:     final currentUid = FirebaseAuth.instance.currentUser?.uid;
  65:     final isOwner = currentUid == appointment.customerId;
  66:     return Scaffold(
  67:       appBar: CustomAppBar(
  68:         title: 'Detalhes do Agendamento',
  69:         showBackButton: true,
  70:       ),
  71:       body: SingleChildScrollView(
  72:         padding: const EdgeInsets.all(
  73:             AppDimensions.screenPaddingHorizontal),
  74:         child: Column(
  75:           crossAxisAlignment: CrossAxisAlignment.stretch,
  76:           children: [
  77:             const SizedBox(height: AppDimensions.paddingLarge),
  78:             // Banner de modo offline
  79:             if (!isOnline)
  80:               Container(
  81:                 margin: const EdgeInsets.only(
  82:                     bottom: AppDimensions.paddingMedium),
  83:                 padding: const EdgeInsets.symmetric(
  84:                     horizontal: 12, vertical: 8),
  85:                 decoration: BoxDecoration(
  86:                   color: Colors.orange.withValues(alpha: 0.12),
  87:                   borderRadius: BorderRadius.circular(8),
  88:                   border: Border.all(color: Colors.orange, width: 1),
  89:                 ),
  90:                 child: const Row(
  91:                   children: [
  92:                     Icon(Icons.wifi_off,
  93:                         color: Colors.orange, size: 16),
  94:                     SizedBox(width: 8),
  95:                     Expanded(
  96:                       child: Text(
  97:                         'Modo offline — cancelamento indisponível.',
  98:                         style: TextStyle(
  99:                             fontSize: 12, color: Colors.orange),
 100:                       ),
 101:                     ),
 102:                   ],
 103:                 ),
 104:               ),
 105:             // Badge de status centralizado
 106:             Center(
 107:               child: Container(
 108:                 padding: const EdgeInsets.symmetric(
 109:                     horizontal: 20, vertical: 6),
 110:                 decoration: BoxDecoration(
 111:                   color: statusInfo.$2.withValues(alpha: 0.15),
 112:                   borderRadius: BorderRadius.circular(20),
 113:                 ),
 114:                 child: Text(
 115:                   statusInfo.$1,
 116:                   style: TextStyle(
 117:                     color: statusInfo.$2,
 118:                     fontSize: 14,
 119:                     fontWeight: FontWeight.bold,
 120:                   ),
 121:                 ),
 122:               ),
 123:             ),
 124:             const SizedBox(height: AppDimensions.paddingLarge),
 125:             Card(
 126:               shape: RoundedRectangleBorder(
 127:                 borderRadius:
 128:                     BorderRadius.circular(AppDimensions.radiusLarge),
 129:               ),
 130:               child: Padding(
 131:                 padding:
 132:                     const EdgeInsets.all(AppDimensions.paddingLarge),
 133:                 child: Column(
 134:                   crossAxisAlignment: CrossAxisAlignment.stretch,
 135:                   children: [
 136:                     // ── Serviço ──────────────────────────────────
 137:                     _sectionTitle('Serviço'),
 138:                     const Divider(),
 139:                     _row(context, 'Filial', resolvedBranchName),
 140:                     _row(context, 'Serviço', resolvedServiceName),
 141:                     _row(context, 'Data',
 142:                         dateFormat.format(appointment.appointmentDate)),
 143:                     _row(context, 'Horário',
 144:                         timeFormat.format(appointment.appointmentDate)),
 145:                     _row(
 146:                       context,
 147:                       'Valor',
 148:                       servicePrice != null
 149:                           ? formatBrl(servicePrice)
 150:                           : '—',
 151:                     ),
 152:                     // ── Veículo ───────────────────────────────────
 153:                     if (isOwner) ...[
 154:                       const SizedBox(
 155:                           height: AppDimensions.paddingMedium),
 156:                       _sectionTitle('Veículo'),
 157:                       const Divider(),
 158:                       _row(
 159:                         context,
 160:                         'Placa',
 161:                         vehiclePlate != null
 162:                             ? formatPlate(vehiclePlate)
 163:                             : '—',
 164:                       ),
 165:                     ],
 166:                     // ── Consultor ─────────────────────────────────
 167:                     if (appointment.consultantName.isNotEmpty) ...[
 168:                       const SizedBox(
 169:                           height: AppDimensions.paddingMedium),
 170:                       _sectionTitle('Consultor'),
 171:                       const Divider(),
 172:                       _row(context, 'Nome',
 173:                           appointment.consultantName),
 174:                       _row(
 175:                         context,
 176:                         'Telefone',
 177:                         appointment.consultantPhone.isNotEmpty
 178:                             ? formatPhone(appointment.consultantPhone)
 179:                             : '—',
 180:                       ),
 181:                     ],
 182:                     // ── Identificação ─────────────────────────────
 183:                     const SizedBox(
 184:                         height: AppDimensions.paddingMedium),
 185:                     _sectionTitle('Identificação'),

 189:                 ),

 200:                           ? AppColors.error
 201:                           : AppColors.grey400),

 206:                     ? 'Cancelar agendamento'
 207:                     : 'Cancelar agendamento (requer internet)'),

 210:             ],

 212:           ],
 213:         ),
 214:       ),
 215:     );
 216:   }
 217:   Widget _sectionTitle(String title) {
 218:     return Padding(
 219:       padding:
 220:           const EdgeInsets.only(bottom: AppDimensions.paddingSmall),
 221:       child: Text(
 222:         title,
 223:         textAlign: TextAlign.center,
 224:         style: const TextStyle(
 225:           fontWeight: FontWeight.bold,
 226:           fontSize: 16,
 227:         ),
 228:       ),
 229:     );
 230:   }
 231:   Widget _row(BuildContext context, String label, String value) {
 232:     return Padding(
 233:       padding: const EdgeInsets.symmetric(
 234:           vertical: AppDimensions.paddingSmall / 2),
 235:       child: Row(
 236:         mainAxisAlignment: MainAxisAlignment.spaceBetween,
 237:         children: [
 238:           Text(label,
 239:               style: Theme.of(context)
 240:                   .textTheme
 241:                   .bodyMedium
 242:                   ?.copyWith(color: AppColors.grey600)),
 243:           Flexible(
 244:             child: Text(
 245:               value,
 246:               textAlign: TextAlign.end,
 247:               style: Theme.of(context)
 248:                   .textTheme
 249:                   .bodyMedium
 250:                   ?.copyWith(fontWeight: FontWeight.bold),
 251:             ),
 252:           ),
 253:         ],
 254:       ),
 255:     );
 256:   }
 257:   Future<void> _tryCancel(BuildContext context) async {
 258:     final creditRepo =
 259:         CreditRepository(FirebaseService().firestore);
 260:     bool limitReached = false;
 261:     int maxCredits = 2;
 262:     maxCredits = await creditRepo.getMaxCredits();
 263:     limitReached =
 264:         await creditRepo.hasReachedLimit(appointment.customerId);
 265:     if (limitReached) {
 266:       if (context.mounted) {
 267:         showDialog(
 268:           context: context,
 269:           builder: (_) => AlertDialog(
 270:             title: const Text('Cancelamento bloqueado'),
 271:             content: Text(
 272:               'Voce ja tem $maxCredits credito(s) ativo(s) — '
 273:               'limite maximo atingido.\n\n'
 274:               'Use seus creditos em novos agendamentos antes de '
 275:               'cancelar este.',
 276:             ),
 277:             actions: [
 278:               FilledButton(
 279:                 onPressed: () => Navigator.pop(context),
 280:                 child: const Text('Entendi'),
 281:               ),
 282:             ],
 283:           ),
 284:         );
 285:       }
 286:       return;
 287:     }
 288:     if (!context.mounted) return;
 289:     final confirm = await showDialog<bool>(
 290:       context: context,
 291:       builder: (_) => AlertDialog(
 292:         title: const Text('Cancelar agendamento'),
 293:         content: const Text(
 294:           'Tem certeza? Um credito sera gerado automaticamente '
 295:           'para uso em novo agendamento nesta filial.',
 296:         ),
 297:         actions: [
 298:           TextButton(
 299:             onPressed: () => Navigator.pop(context, false),
 300:             child: const Text('Voltar'),
 301:           ),
 302:           FilledButton(
 303:             style: FilledButton.styleFrom(
 304:                 backgroundColor: AppColors.error),
 305:             onPressed: () => Navigator.pop(context, true),
 306:             child: const Text('Cancelar agendamento'),
 307:           ),
 308:         ],
 309:       ),
 310:     );
 311:     if (confirm == true) {
 312:       try {
 313:         await AppointmentRepository(FirebaseService().firestore)
 314:             .cancelAppointment(appointment, customerName);
 315:         onCanceled();
 316:         if (context.mounted) {
 317:           ScaffoldMessenger.of(context).showSnackBar(
 318:             const SnackBar(
 319:               content: Text(
 320:                 'Agendamento cancelado. Credito gerado para novo agendamento.',
 321:               ),
 322:             ),
 323:           );
 324:           Navigator.of(context).pop();
 325:         }
 326:       } catch (e) {
 327:         if (context.mounted) {
 328:           ScaffoldMessenger.of(context).showSnackBar(
 329:             SnackBar(content: Text('Erro ao cancelar: $e')),
 330:           );
 331:         }
 332:       }
 333:     }
 334:   }
 335:   (String, Color) _statusInfo(String status) {
 336:     return switch (status) {
 337:       'confirmed' => ('Confirmado', AppColors.success),
 338:       'completed' => ('Concluido', AppColors.info),
 339:       'canceled' => ('Cancelado', AppColors.error),
 340:       _ => ('Pendente', AppColors.warning),
 341:     };
 342:   }
 343: }

   1: import 'package:cloud_firestore/cloud_firestore.dart';
   2: import 'package:firebase_auth/firebase_auth.dart';
