   7: import '../../data/repositories/user_repository.dart';
   8: class AuthScreen extends StatefulWidget {
   9:   const AuthScreen({super.key});
  10:   @override
  11:   State<AuthScreen> createState() => _AuthScreenState();
  12: }
  13: class _AuthScreenState extends State<AuthScreen> {
  14:   final _formKey = GlobalKey<FormState>();
  15:   final _nameCtrl = TextEditingController();
  16:   final _emailLoginCtrl = TextEditingController();
  17:   final _emailRegisterCtrl = TextEditingController();
  18:   final _identifierCtrl = TextEditingController();
  19:   final _passCtrl = TextEditingController();
  20:   bool _isLogin = true;
  21:   bool _loading = false;
  22:   bool _passVisible = false;
  23:   // 'email' | 'cpf' | 'phone'
  24:   String _identifierType = 'cpf';
  25:   @override
  26:   void dispose() {
  27:     _nameCtrl.dispose();
  28:     _emailLoginCtrl.dispose();
  29:     _emailRegisterCtrl.dispose();
  30:     _identifierCtrl.dispose();
  31:     _passCtrl.dispose();
  32:     super.dispose();
  33:   }
  34:   String _identifierLabel() {
  35:     switch (_identifierType) {
  36:       case 'cpf':
  37:         return 'CPF';
  38:       case 'phone':
  39:         return 'Telefone';
  40:       default:
  41:         return 'E-mail';
  42:     }
  43:   }
  44:   IconData _identifierIcon() {
  45:     switch (_identifierType) {
  46:       case 'cpf':
  47:         return Icons.badge_outlined;
  48:       case 'phone':
  49:         return Icons.phone_outlined;
  50:       default:
  51:         return Icons.email_outlined;
  52:     }
  53:   }
  54:   TextInputType _identifierKeyboard() {
  55:     switch (_identifierType) {
  56:       case 'cpf':
  57:       case 'phone':
  58:         return TextInputType.number;
  59:       default:
  60:         return TextInputType.emailAddress;
  61:     }
  62:   }
  63:   String? _validateIdentifier(String? v) {
  64:     if (v == null || v.trim().isEmpty) {
  65:       return 'Informe seu ${_identifierLabel()}';
  66:     }
  67:     if (_identifierType == 'cpf') {
  68:       final digits = v.replaceAll(RegExp(r'[^0-9]'), '');
  69:       if (digits.length != 11) return 'CPF deve ter 11 digitos';
  70:     }
  71:     if (_identifierType == 'phone') {
  72:       final digits = v.replaceAll(RegExp(r'[^0-9]'), '');
  73:       if (digits.length < 10) return 'Telefone invalido';
  74:     }
  75:     if (_identifierType == 'email') {
  76:       if (!v.contains('@')) return 'E-mail invalido';
  77:     }
  78:     return null;
  79:   }
  80:   /// Busca o email real na coleção pública `identifiers`.
  81:   Future<String?> _getEmailByIdentifier(String identifier) async {
  82:     final snap = await FirebaseFirestore.instance
  83:         .collection('identifiers')
  84:         .doc(identifier.trim().toLowerCase())
  85:         .get();
  86:     if (snap.exists) {
  87:       return snap.data()?['email'] as String?;
  88:     }
  89:     return null;
  90:   }
  91:   /// Login com e-mail direto (sem lookup em identifiers).
  92:   Future<void> _submitEmailLogin() async {
  93:     if (!_formKey.currentState!.validate()) return;
  94:     setState(() => _loading = true);
  95:     try {
  96:       await FirebaseAuth.instance.signInWithEmailAndPassword(
  97:         email: _emailLoginCtrl.text.trim(),
  98:         password: _passCtrl.text.trim(),
  99:       );
 100:     } on FirebaseAuthException catch (e) {
 101:       if (!mounted) return;
 102:       final msg = switch (e.code) {
 103:         'user-not-found' => 'E-mail nao encontrado.',
 104:         'wrong-password' => 'Senha incorreta.',
 105:         'invalid-credential' => 'E-mail ou senha incorretos.',
 106:         _ => e.message ?? 'Erro de autenticacao.',
 107:       };
 108:       ScaffoldMessenger.of(context).showSnackBar(SnackBar(content: Text(msg)));
 109:     } catch (e) {
 110:       if (mounted) {
 111:         ScaffoldMessenger.of(context)
 112:             .showSnackBar(SnackBar(content: Text('Erro: $e')));
 113:       }
 114:     } finally {
 115:       if (mounted) setState(() => _loading = false);
 116:     }
 117:   }
 118:   /// Login via CPF ou Telefone (lookup em identifiers).
 119:   Future<void> _submitIdentifierLogin() async {
 120:     if (!_formKey.currentState!.validate()) return;
 121:     setState(() => _loading = true);
 122:     try {
 123:       final identifier = _identifierCtrl.text.trim();
 124:       final email = await _getEmailByIdentifier(identifier);
 125:       if (email == null) {
 126:         if (mounted) {
 127:           ScaffoldMessenger.of(context).showSnackBar(
 128:             const SnackBar(content: Text('Identificador nao encontrado.')),
 129:           );
 130:         }
 131:         return;
 132:       }
 133:       await FirebaseAuth.instance.signInWithEmailAndPassword(
 134:         email: email,
 135:         password: _passCtrl.text.trim(),
 136:       );
 137:     } on FirebaseAuthException catch (e) {
 138:       if (!mounted) return;
 139:       final msg = switch (e.code) {
 140:         'wrong-password' => 'Senha incorreta.',
 141:         'invalid-credential' => 'Identificador ou senha incorretos.',
 142:         _ => e.message ?? 'Erro de autenticacao.',
 143:       };
 144:       ScaffoldMessenger.of(context).showSnackBar(SnackBar(content: Text(msg)));
 145:     } catch (e) {
 146:       if (mounted) {
 147:         ScaffoldMessenger.of(context)
 148:             .showSnackBar(SnackBar(content: Text('Erro: $e')));
 149:       }
 150:     } finally {
 151:       if (mounted) setState(() => _loading = false);
 152:     }
 153:   }
 154:   /// Cadastro novo usuário.
 155:   Future<void> _submitRegister() async {
 156:     if (!_formKey.currentState!.validate()) return;
 157:     setState(() => _loading = true);
 158:     try {
 159:       final auth = FirebaseAuth.instance;
 160:       final identifier = _identifierCtrl.text.trim();
 161:       final email = _identifierType == 'email'
 162:           ? identifier
 163:           : _emailRegisterCtrl.text.trim();
 164:       final cred = await auth.createUserWithEmailAndPassword(
 165:         email: email,
 166:         password: _passCtrl.text.trim(),
 167:       );
 168:       await UserRepository(FirebaseFirestore.instance).createUser(
 169:         UserModel(
 170:           uid: cred.user!.uid,
 171:           name: _nameCtrl.text.trim(),
 172:           email: email,
 173:           role: 'user',
 174:           identifier: identifier.toLowerCase(),
 175:           identifierType: _identifierType,
 176:         ),
 177:       );
 178:       final key = identifier.trim().toLowerCase();
 179:       await FirebaseFirestore.instance
 180:           .collection('identifiers')
 181:           .doc(key)
 182:           .set({'email': email, 'identifier_type': _identifierType});
 183:     } on FirebaseAuthException catch (e) {
 184:       if (!mounted) return;
 185:       final msg = switch (e.code) {
 186:         'email-already-in-use' => 'Este e-mail ja esta cadastrado.',
 187:         'weak-password' => 'Senha fraca — minimo 6 caracteres.',
 188:         _ => e.message ?? 'Erro de autenticacao.',
 189:       };
 190:       ScaffoldMessenger.of(context).showSnackBar(SnackBar(content: Text(msg)));
 191:     } catch (e) {
 192:       if (mounted) {
 193:         ScaffoldMessenger.of(context)
 194:             .showSnackBar(SnackBar(content: Text('Erro: $e')));
 195:       }
 196:     } finally {
 197:       if (mounted) setState(() => _loading = false);
 198:     }
 199:   }
 200:   /// Login / cadastro com Google.
 201:   Future<void> _signInWithGoogle() async {
 202:     setState(() => _loading = true);
 203:     try {
 204:       final googleUser = await GoogleSignIn().signIn();
 205:       if (googleUser == null) return; // usuário cancelou
 206:       final googleAuth = await googleUser.authentication;
 207:       final credential = GoogleAuthProvider.credential(
 208:         accessToken: googleAuth.accessToken,
 209:         idToken: googleAuth.idToken,
 210:       );
 211:       final userCred =
 212:           await FirebaseAuth.instance.signInWithCredential(credential);
 213:       final user = userCred.user!;
 214:       // Se for o primeiro login com Google, cria o documento no Firestore
 215:       final isNew = userCred.additionalUserInfo?.isNewUser ?? false;
 216:       if (isNew) {
 217:         final email = user.email ?? '';
 218:         final name = user.displayName ?? '';
 219:         await UserRepository(FirebaseFirestore.instance).createUser(
 220:           UserModel(
 221:             uid: user.uid,
 222:             name: name,
 223:             email: email,
 224:             role: 'user',
 225:             identifier: email.toLowerCase(),
 226:             identifierType: 'email',
 227:           ),
 228:         );
 229:         await FirebaseFirestore.instance
 230:             .collection('identifiers')
 231:             .doc(email.toLowerCase())
 232:             .set({'email': email, 'identifier_type': 'email'});
 233:       }
 234:     } on FirebaseAuthException catch (e) {
 235:       if (!mounted) return;
 236:       ScaffoldMessenger.of(context).showSnackBar(
 237:         SnackBar(content: Text(e.message ?? 'Erro ao entrar com Google.')),
 238:       );
 239:     } catch (e) {
 240:       if (mounted) {
 241:         ScaffoldMessenger.of(context)
 242:             .showSnackBar(SnackBar(content: Text('Erro: $e')));
 243:       }
 244:     } finally {
 245:       if (mounted) setState(() => _loading = false);
 246:     }
 247:   }
 248:   Future<void> _forgotPassword() async {
 249:     // Mostra campos distintos dependendo do tipo de identificador
 250:     final identifierCtrl = TextEditingController(
 251:       text: _identifierType == 'email'
 252:           ? _emailLoginCtrl.text.trim()
 253:           : _identifierCtrl.text.trim(),
 254:     );
 255:     final confirmed = await showDialog<bool>(
 256:       context: context,
 257:       builder: (ctx) => AlertDialog(
 258:         title: const Text('Redefinir senha'),
 259:         content: Column(
 260:           mainAxisSize: MainAxisSize.min,
 261:           crossAxisAlignment: CrossAxisAlignment.start,
 262:           children: [
 263:             const Text(
 264:               'Digite o identificador cadastrado.\n'
 265:               'Enviaremos um link de redefinição para o e-mail associado.',
 266:               style: TextStyle(fontSize: 13),
 267:             ),
 268:             const SizedBox(height: 16),
 269:             TextField(
 270:               controller: identifierCtrl,
 271:               keyboardType: _identifierKeyboard(),
 272:               autofocus: true,
 273:               decoration: InputDecoration(
 274:                 labelText: _identifierLabel(),
 275:                 prefixIcon: Icon(_identifierIcon()),
 276:               ),
 277:             ),
 278:           ],
 279:         ),
 280:         actions: [
 281:           TextButton(
 282:             onPressed: () => Navigator.pop(ctx, false),
 283:             child: const Text('Cancelar'),
 284:           ),
 285:           FilledButton(
 286:             onPressed: () => Navigator.pop(ctx, true),
 287:             child: const Text('Enviar link'),
 288:           ),
 289:         ],
 290:       ),
 291:     );
 292:     if (confirmed != true) return;
 293:     final identifier = identifierCtrl.text.trim();
 294:     identifierCtrl.dispose();
 295:     if (identifier.isEmpty) return;
 296:     setState(() => _loading = true);
 297:     try {
 298:       String? email;
 299:       if (_identifierType == 'email') {
 300:         email = identifier;
 301:       } else {
 302:         email = await _getEmailByIdentifier(identifier);
 303:       }
 304:       if (email == null) {
 305:         if (mounted) {
 306:           ScaffoldMessenger.of(context).showSnackBar(
 307:             const SnackBar(content: Text('Identificador nao encontrado.')),
 308:           );
 309:         }
 310:         return;
 311:       }
 312:       await FirebaseAuth.instance.sendPasswordResetEmail(email: email);
 313:       if (mounted) {
 314:         ScaffoldMessenger.of(context).showSnackBar(
 315:           const SnackBar(
 316:             content: Text(
 317:                 'Link de redefinicao enviado para o e-mail cadastrado.'),
 318:             duration: Duration(seconds: 4),
 319:           ),
 320:         );
 321:       }
 322:     } on FirebaseAuthException catch (e) {
 323:       if (mounted) {
 324:         ScaffoldMessenger.of(context).showSnackBar(
 325:           SnackBar(content: Text(e.message ?? 'Erro ao enviar e-mail.')),
 326:         );
 327:       }
 328:     } catch (e) {
 329:       if (mounted) {
 330:         ScaffoldMessenger.of(context)
 331:             .showSnackBar(SnackBar(content: Text('Erro: $e')));
 332:       }
 333:     } finally {
 334:       if (mounted) setState(() => _loading = false);
 335:     }
 336:   }
 337:   void _switchMode() {

 339:       _isLogin = !_isLogin;

 341:       _nameCtrl.clear();
 342:       _emailLoginCtrl.clear();
 343:       _emailRegisterCtrl.clear();
 344:       _identifierCtrl.clear();
 345:       _passCtrl.clear();

   1: import 'package:flutter/material.dart';
   2: import 'package:flutter_riverpod/flutter_riverpod.dart';
   3: import 'package:lavamax/core/constants/app_dimensions.dart';
   4: import 'package:lavamax/core/constants/app_strings.dart';
   5: import 'package:lavamax/presentation/providers/branch_provider.dart';
   6: import 'package:lavamax/presentation/providers/consultant_provider.dart';
   7: import 'package:lavamax/presentation/providers/service_provider.dart';
   8: import 'package:lavamax/presentation/providers/slot_provider.dart';
   9: import 'package:lavamax/presentation/providers/vehicle_provider.dart';
  10: import 'package:lavamax/presentation/screens/service_selection_screen.dart';
  11: import 'package:lavamax/presentation/widgets/branch_card.dart';
  12: import 'package:lavamax/presentation/widgets/custom_app_bar.dart';
  13: class BranchSelectionScreen extends ConsumerWidget {
  14:   const BranchSelectionScreen({super.key});
  15:   @override
  16:   Widget build(BuildContext context, WidgetRef ref) {
  17:     final branchesAsync = ref.watch(branchesProvider);
  18:     final selectedVehicle = ref.watch(selectedVehicleProvider);
  19:     return Scaffold(
  20:       appBar: CustomAppBar(
  21:         title: AppStrings.selectBranch,
  22:         showBackButton: true,
  23:       ),
  24:       body: branchesAsync.when(
  25:         data: (branches) {
  26:           // Filtra filiais pela marca do veículo selecionado.
  27:           // Regra: se a filial tem `allowedBrand`, só aparece se o veículo
  28:           // for daquela marca. Filiais sem restrição aparecem sempre.
  29:           final vehicleBrand = selectedVehicle?.brand.toLowerCase() ?? '';
  30:           final filtered = branches.where((b) {
  31:             if (b.allowedBrand == null) return true;
  32:             return vehicleBrand == b.allowedBrand!.toLowerCase();
  33:           }).toList();
  34:           if (filtered.isEmpty) {
  35:             return const Center(
  36:               child: Text('Nenhuma filial disponível para este veículo.'),
  37:             );
  38:           }
  39:           return ListView.builder(
  40:             padding: const EdgeInsets.all(AppDimensions.screenPaddingHorizontal),
  41:             itemCount: filtered.length,
  42:             itemBuilder: (context, index) {
  43:               final branch = filtered[index];
  44:               return Padding(
  45:                 padding: const EdgeInsets.only(
  46:                     bottom: AppDimensions.paddingMedium),
  47:                 child: BranchCard(
  48:                   branch: branch,
  49:                   onTap: () {
  50:                     ref.read(selectedBranchProvider.notifier).state = branch;
  51:                     // Reseta apenas serviço/slot/consultor — veículo já foi escolhido
  52:                     ref.read(selectedServiceProvider.notifier).state = null;
  53:                     ref.read(selectedDateProvider.notifier).state = null;
  54:                     ref.read(selectedSlotProvider.notifier).state = null;
  55:                     ref.read(selectedConsultantProvider.notifier).state = null;
  56:                     ref.read(consultantHasConflictProvider.notifier).state =
  57:                         false;
  58:                     Navigator.of(context).push(
  59:                       MaterialPageRoute(
  60:                         builder: (_) => const ServiceSelectionScreen(),
  61:                       ),
  62:                     );
  63:                   },
  64:                 ),
  65:               );
  66:             },
  67:           );
  68:         },
  69:         loading: () => const Center(child: CircularProgressIndicator()),
  70:         error: (error, stackTrace) =>
  71:             Center(child: Text('Erro: $error')),
  72:       ),
  73:     );
  74:   }
  75: }

==================================================

   2: import 'package:flutter/services.dart';
   3: import 'package:lavamax/core/constants/app_colors.dart';
   4: import 'package:lavamax/data/models/vehicle_brand_model.dart';
   5: /// Tela de seleção de marca com lista completa e índice alfabético lateral.

   7: class BrandSelectionScreen extends StatefulWidget {
   8:   final List<VehicleBrandModel> brands;

  12: }
  13: class _BrandSelectionScreenState extends State<BrandSelectionScreen> {
  14:   final _scrollController = ScrollController();
  15:   final _searchController = TextEditingController();
  16:   // letra atualmente destacada no índice
  17:   String? _activeLetter;
  18:   // brands filtradas pela busca
  19:   late List<VehicleBrandModel> _filtered;
  20:   // mapa letra → GlobalKey do cabeçalho da seção
  21:   final Map<String, GlobalKey> _sectionKeys = {};
  22:   // letras presentes nas marcas filtradas (em ordem)
  23:   List<String> _letters = [];
  24:   @override
  25:   void initState() {
  26:     super.initState();
  27:     _filtered = List.of(widget.brands);
  28:     _rebuildIndex();
  29:   }
  30:   @override
  31:   void dispose() {
  32:     _scrollController.dispose();
  33:     _searchController.dispose();
  34:     super.dispose();
  35:   }
  36:   // ── helpers ────────────────────────────────────────────────
  37:   void _rebuildIndex() {
  38:     _sectionKeys.clear();
  39:     final lettersSet = <String>{};
  40:     for (final b in _filtered) {
  41:       if (b.name.isEmpty) continue;
  42:       final l = b.name[0].toUpperCase();
  43:       lettersSet.add(l);
  44:     }
  45:     _letters = lettersSet.toList()..sort();
  46:     for (final l in _letters) {
  47:       _sectionKeys[l] = GlobalKey();
  48:     }
  49:   }
  50:   void _onSearch(String query) {
  51:     setState(() {
  52:       final q = query.trim().toLowerCase();
  53:       _filtered = q.isEmpty
  54:           ? List.of(widget.brands)
  55:           : widget.brands
  56:               .where((b) => b.name.toLowerCase().contains(q))
  57:               .toList();
  58:       _rebuildIndex();
  59:       _activeLetter = null;
  60:     });
  61:   }
  62:   void _scrollToLetter(String letter) {
  63:     final key = _sectionKeys[letter];
  64:     if (key == null) return;
  65:     final ctx = key.currentContext;
  66:     if (ctx == null) return;
  67:     HapticFeedback.selectionClick();
  68:     setState(() => _activeLetter = letter);
  69:     Scrollable.ensureVisible(
  70:       ctx,
  71:       duration: const Duration(milliseconds: 300),
  72:       curve: Curves.easeOut,
  73:       alignment: 0.0,
  74:     );
  75:   }
  76:   // ── build ──────────────────────────────────────────────────
  77:   @override
  78:   Widget build(BuildContext context) {
  79:     // agrupa marcas por letra
  80:     final Map<String, List<VehicleBrandModel>> grouped = {};
  81:     for (final b in _filtered) {
  82:       if (b.name.isEmpty) continue;
  83:       final l = b.name[0].toUpperCase();
  84:       grouped.putIfAbsent(l, () => []).add(b);
  85:     }
  86:     return Scaffold(
  87:       appBar: AppBar(
  88:         title: const Text('Selecione a Marca'),
  89:         bottom: PreferredSize(
  90:           preferredSize: const Size.fromHeight(56),
  91:           child: Padding(
  92:             padding:
  93:                 const EdgeInsets.symmetric(horizontal: 16, vertical: 8),
  94:             child: TextField(
  95:               controller: _searchController,
  96:               autofocus: true,
  97:               onChanged: _onSearch,
  98:               decoration: InputDecoration(
  99:                 hintText: 'Buscar marca…',
 100:                 prefixIcon: const Icon(Icons.search),
 101:                 suffixIcon: _searchController.text.isNotEmpty
 102:                     ? IconButton(
 103:                         icon: const Icon(Icons.clear),
 104:                         onPressed: () {
 105:                           _searchController.clear();
 106:                           _onSearch('');
 107:                         },
 108:                       )
 109:                     : null,
 110:                 isDense: true,
 111:                 filled: true,
 112:                 fillColor: Theme.of(context).colorScheme.surface,
 113:                 border: OutlineInputBorder(
 114:                   borderRadius: BorderRadius.circular(12),
 115:                   borderSide: BorderSide.none,
 116:                 ),
 117:               ),
 118:             ),
 119:           ),
 120:         ),
 121:       ),
 122:       body: _filtered.isEmpty
 123:           ? const Center(child: Text('Nenhuma marca encontrada.'))
 124:           : Stack(
 125:               children: [
 126:                 // ── Lista principal ──────────────────────────
 127:                 ListView.builder(
 128:                   controller: _scrollController,
 129:                   // margem direita para não sobrepor o índice
 130:                   padding: const EdgeInsets.only(right: 32),
 131:                   itemCount: _letters.length,
 132:                   itemBuilder: (_, i) {
 133:                     final letter = _letters[i];
 134:                     final items = grouped[letter] ?? [];
 135:                     return Column(
 136:                       crossAxisAlignment: CrossAxisAlignment.start,
 137:                       children: [
 138:                         // cabeçalho da seção
 139:                         Container(
 140:                           key: _sectionKeys[letter],
 141:                           width: double.infinity,
 142:                           color: AppColors.grey100,
 143:                           padding: const EdgeInsets.symmetric(
 144:                             horizontal: 16,
 145:                             vertical: 6,
 146:                           ),
 147:                           child: Text(
 148:                             letter,
 149:                             style: TextStyle(
 150:                               fontWeight: FontWeight.bold,
 151:                               fontSize: 13,
 152:                               color: AppColors.grey700,
 153:                             ),
 154:                           ),
 155:                         ),
 156:                         // itens da seção
 157:                         ...items.map(
 158:                           (brand) => ListTile(
 159:                             leading: const Icon(
 160:                               Icons.directions_car_outlined,
 161:                               color: AppColors.grey500,
 162:                             ),
 163:                             title: Text(brand.name),
 164:                             onTap: () => Navigator.of(context).pop(brand),
 165:                           ),
 166:                         ),
 167:                       ],
 168:                     );
 169:                   },
 170:                 ),
 171:                 // ── Índice alfabético lateral ────────────────
 172:                 if (_searchController.text.isEmpty)
 173:                   Positioned(
 174:                     right: 0,
 175:                     top: 0,
 176:                     bottom: 0,
 177:                     child: _AlphabetIndex(
 178:                       letters: _letters,
 179:                       activeLetter: _activeLetter,
 180:                       onLetterTap: _scrollToLetter,
 181:                     ),
 182:                   ),
 183:               ],
 184:             ),
 185:     );
 186:   }
 187: }
 188: // ── Widget do índice lateral ────────────────────────────────
 189: class _AlphabetIndex extends StatelessWidget {
 190:   final List<String> letters;
 191:   final String? activeLetter;
 192:   final ValueChanged<String> onLetterTap;
 193:   const _AlphabetIndex({
 194:     required this.letters,
 195:     required this.activeLetter,
 196:     required this.onLetterTap,
 197:   });
 198:   @override
 199:   Widget build(BuildContext context) {
 200:     return GestureDetector(
 201:       // arrasto contínuo sobre o índice
 202:       onVerticalDragUpdate: (details) {
 203:         final box = context.findRenderObject() as RenderBox?;
 204:         if (box == null) return;
 205:         final localY = box.globalToLocal(details.globalPosition).dy;
 206:         final itemHeight = box.size.height / letters.length;
 207:         final idx = (localY / itemHeight).floor().clamp(0, letters.length - 1);
 208:         onLetterTap(letters[idx]);
 209:       },
 210:       child: Container(
 211:         width: 28,
 212:         decoration: BoxDecoration(
 213:           color: AppColors.grey100.withValues(alpha: 0.9),
 214:           borderRadius: const BorderRadius.only(
 215:             topLeft: Radius.circular(8),
 216:             bottomLeft: Radius.circular(8),
 217:           ),
 218:         ),
 219:         child: Column(
 220:           mainAxisAlignment: MainAxisAlignment.center,
 221:           children: letters.map((l) {
 222:             final isActive = l == activeLetter;
 223:             return GestureDetector(
 224:               onTap: () => onLetterTap(l),
 225:               child: Container(
 226:                 width: 28,
 227:                 height: 22,
 228:                 alignment: Alignment.center,
 229:                 decoration: isActive
 230:                     ? const BoxDecoration(
 231:                         color: AppColors.accent,
 232:                         shape: BoxShape.circle,
 233:                       )
 234:                     : null,
 235:                 child: Text(
 236:                   l,
 237:                   style: TextStyle(
 238:                     fontSize: 11,
 239:                     fontWeight: FontWeight.bold,
 240:                     color: isActive ? AppColors.white : AppColors.grey700,
 241:                   ),
 242:                 ),
 243:               ),
 244:             );
 245:           }).toList(),
 246:         ),
 247:       ),
 248:     );
 249:   }
 250: }

  15: final _activeCreditsProvider = FutureProvider.autoDispose<int>((ref) async {
  16:   final uid = FirebaseAuth.instance.currentUser?.uid;
  17:   if (uid == null) return 0;
  18:   final snap = await FirebaseService().firestore
  19:       .collection('credits')
  20:       .where('customer_id', isEqualTo: uid)
  21:       .where('status', isEqualTo: 'active')
  22:       .get();
  23:   return snap.docs.length;
  24: });

  20: class MyAppointmentsScreen extends ConsumerWidget {

  34:       );
  35:     }
  36:     final isOnline = ref.watch(isOnlineProvider);
  37:     final appointmentsAsync =
  38:         ref.watch(customerAppointmentsProvider(currentUser.uid));
  39:     final userAsync = ref.watch(userRoleProvider);
  40:     final customerName = userAsync.when(
  41:       data: (u) => u?.name ?? '',
  42:       loading: () => '',
  43:       error: (_, _) => '',
  44:     );
  45:     final branchesAsync = ref.watch(branchesProvider);
  46:     final servicesAsync = ref.watch(servicesProvider);
  47:     final vehiclesAsync = ref.watch(userVehiclesProvider);
  48:     return Scaffold(
  49:       appBar: CustomAppBar(
  50:         title: 'Meus Agendamentos',
  51:         showBackButton: true,
  52:       ),
  53:       body: Column(
  54:         children: [
  55:           if (!isOnline)
  56:             Container(
  57:               width: double.infinity,
  58:               color: Colors.orange.withValues(alpha: 0.12),
  59:               padding: const EdgeInsets.symmetric(
  60:                 horizontal: 16,
  61:                 vertical: 10,
  62:               ),
  63:               child: const Row(
  64:                 children: [
  65:                   Icon(Icons.wifi_off, color: Colors.orange, size: 16),
  66:                   SizedBox(width: 10),
  67:                   Expanded(
  68:                     child: Text(
  69:                       'Modo offline — exibindo dados salvos. '
  70:                       'Cancelamentos requerem internet.',
  71:                       style: TextStyle(
  72:                         fontSize: 12,
  73:                         color: Colors.orange,
  74:                       ),
  75:                     ),
  76:                   ),
  77:                 ],
  78:               ),
  79:             ),
  80:           Expanded(
  81:             child: appointmentsAsync.when(
  82:               data: (appointments) {
  83:                 if (appointments.isEmpty) {
  84:                   return const Center(
  85:                     child: Column(
  86:                       mainAxisAlignment: MainAxisAlignment.center,
  87:                       children: [
  88:                         Icon(
  89:                           Icons.calendar_today_outlined,
  90:                           size: 64,
  91:                           color: AppColors.grey400,
  92:                         ),
  93:                         SizedBox(height: 16),
  94:                         Text(
  95:                           'Nenhum agendamento encontrado.',
  96:                           style: TextStyle(color: AppColors.grey600),
  97:                         ),
  98:                       ],
  99:                     ),
 100:                   );
 101:                 }
 102:                 return ListView.separated(
 103:                   padding: const EdgeInsets.all(
 104:                     AppDimensions.screenPaddingHorizontal,
 105:                   ),
 106:                   itemCount: appointments.length,
 107:                   separatorBuilder: (_, _) =>
 108:                       const SizedBox(height: AppDimensions.paddingSmall),
 109:                   itemBuilder: (context, index) {
 110:                     return _AppointmentCard(
 111:                       appointment: appointments[index],
 112:                       customerName: customerName,
 113:                       branches: branchesAsync.valueOrNull ?? [],
 114:                       services: servicesAsync.valueOrNull ?? [],
 115:                       vehicles: vehiclesAsync.valueOrNull ?? [],
 116:                       isOnline: isOnline,
 117:                       onChanged: () => ref.invalidate(
 118:                         customerAppointmentsProvider(currentUser.uid),
 119:                       ),
 120:                     );
 121:                   },
 122:                 );
 123:               },
 124:               loading: () =>
 125:                   const Center(child: CircularProgressIndicator()),
 126:               error: (e, _) => Center(
 127:                 child: Column(
 128:                   mainAxisAlignment: MainAxisAlignment.center,
 129:                   children: [
 130:                     const Icon(
 131:                       Icons.cloud_off,
 132:                       size: 48,
 133:                       color: AppColors.grey400,
 134:                     ),
 135:                     const SizedBox(height: 12),
 136:                     Text(
 137:                       isOnline
 138:                           ? 'Erro ao carregar agendamentos.'
 139:                           : 'Sem conexão. Não há dados salvos localmente.',
 140:                       textAlign: TextAlign.center,
 141:                       style: const TextStyle(color: AppColors.grey600),
 142:                     ),
 143:                   ],
 144:                 ),
 145:               ),
 146:             ),
 147:           ),
 148:         ],
 149:       ),
 150:     );
 151:   }
 152: }
 153: class _AppointmentCard extends StatelessWidget {
 154:   const _AppointmentCard({
 155:     required this.appointment,
 156:     required this.customerName,
 157:     required this.branches,
 158:     required this.services,
 159:     required this.vehicles,
 160:     required this.isOnline,
 161:     required this.onChanged,
 162:   });
 163:   final AppointmentModel appointment;
 164:   final String customerName;
 165:   final List<BranchModel> branches;
 166:   final List<ServiceModel> services;
 167:   final List<VehicleModel> vehicles;
 168:   final bool isOnline;
 169:   final VoidCallback onChanged;
 170:   @override
 171:   Widget build(BuildContext context) {
 172:     final dateFormat = DateFormat('dd/MM/yyyy');
 173:     final timeFormat = DateFormat('HH:mm');
 174:     final statusInfo = _statusInfo(appointment.status);
 175:     final branchName = appointment.branchName.isNotEmpty
 176:         ? appointment.branchName
 177:         : _resolveName(
 178:             branches,
 179:             appointment.branchId,
 180:             fallback: appointment.branchId,
 181:           );
 182:     final serviceName = appointment.serviceName.isNotEmpty
 183:         ? appointment.serviceName
 184:         : _resolveName(
 185:             services,
 186:             appointment.serviceId,
 187:             fallback: appointment.serviceId,
 188:           );
 189:     final vehicle = _resolveVehicle(appointment.vehicleId);
 190:     return Card(
 191:       shape: RoundedRectangleBorder(
 192:         borderRadius: BorderRadius.circular(
 193:           AppDimensions.radiusMedium,
 194:         ),
 195:       ),
 196:       child: InkWell(
 197:         borderRadius: BorderRadius.circular(
 198:           AppDimensions.radiusMedium,
 199:         ),
 200:         onTap: () => Navigator.push(
 201:           context,
 202:           MaterialPageRoute(
 203:             builder: (_) => AppointmentDetailScreen(
 204:               appointment: appointment,
 205:               customerName: customerName,
 206:               resolvedBranchName: branchName,
 207:               resolvedServiceName: serviceName,
 208:               isOnline: isOnline,
 209:               onCanceled: onChanged,
 210:             ),
 211:           ),
 212:         ),
 213:         child: Padding(
 214:           padding: const EdgeInsets.all(
 215:             AppDimensions.paddingMedium,
 216:           ),
 217:           child: Column(
 218:             crossAxisAlignment: CrossAxisAlignment.start,
 219:             children: [
 220:               Row(
 221:                 children: [
 222:                   Expanded(
 223:                     child: Column(
 224:                       crossAxisAlignment:
 225:                           CrossAxisAlignment.start,
 226:                       children: [
 227:                         Text(
 228:                           dateFormat.format(
 229:                             appointment.appointmentDate,
 230:                           ),
 231:                           style: Theme.of(context)
 232:                               .textTheme
 233:                               .titleSmall
 234:                               ?.copyWith(
 235:                                 fontWeight: FontWeight.bold,
 236:                               ),
 237:                         ),
 238:                         Text(
 239:                           timeFormat.format(
 240:                             appointment.appointmentDate,
 241:                           ),
 242:                           style: Theme.of(context)
 243:                               .textTheme
 244:                               .bodySmall
 245:                               ?.copyWith(
 246:                                 color: AppColors.grey600,
 247:                               ),
 248:                         ),
 249:                       ],
 250:                     ),
 251:                   ),
 252:                   Container(
 253:                     padding: const EdgeInsets.symmetric(
 254:                       horizontal: 10,
 255:                       vertical: 4,
 256:                     ),
 257:                     decoration: BoxDecoration(
 258:                       color: statusInfo.$2.withValues(
 259:                         alpha: 0.15,
 260:                       ),
 261:                       borderRadius: BorderRadius.circular(20),
 262:                     ),
 263:                     child: Text(
 264:                       statusInfo.$1,
 265:                       style: TextStyle(
 266:                         color: statusInfo.$2,
 267:                         fontSize: 12,
 268:                         fontWeight: FontWeight.bold,
 269:                       ),
 270:                     ),
 271:                   ),
 272:                 ],
 273:               ),
 274:               const Divider(
 275:                 height: AppDimensions.paddingLarge,
 276:               ),
 277:               _infoRow(
 278:                 context,
 279:                 Icons.store_outlined,
 280:                 'Filial: $branchName',
 281:               ),
 282:               const SizedBox(height: 6),
 283:               _infoRow(
 284:                 context,
 285:                 Icons.local_car_wash_outlined,
 286:                 'Serviço: $serviceName',
 287:               ),
 288:               if (appointment.consultantName.isNotEmpty) ...[
 289:                 const SizedBox(height: 6),
 290:                 _infoRow(
 291:                   context,
 292:                   Icons.person_outline,
 293:                   'Consultor: ${appointment.consultantName}',
 294:                 ),
 295:               ],
 296:               if (vehicle != null) ...[
 297:                 const SizedBox(height: 6),
 298:                 _infoRow(
 299:                   context,
 300:                   Icons.pin_outlined,
 301:                   'Placa: ${formatPlate(vehicle.plate)}',
 302:                 ),
 303:               ],
 304:               const SizedBox(height: 6),
 305:               Align(
 306:                 alignment: Alignment.centerRight,
 307:                 child: Text(
 308:                   'Ver detalhes',
 309:                   style: TextStyle(
 310:                     fontSize: 12,
 311:                     color: Theme.of(context)
 312:                         .colorScheme
 313:                         .primary,
 314:                   ),
 315:                 ),
 316:               ),
 317:             ],
 318:           ),
 319:         ),
 320:       ),
 321:     );
 322:   }
 323:   VehicleModel? _resolveVehicle(String vehicleId) {
 324:     try {
 325:       return vehicles.firstWhere((e) => e.id == vehicleId);
 326:     } catch (_) {
 327:       return null;
 328:     }
 329:   }
 330:   String _resolveName<T>(
 331:     List<T> items,
 332:     String id, {
 333:     required String fallback,
 334:   }) {
 335:     try {
 336:       final item = (items as List).firstWhere(
 337:         (e) => (e as dynamic).id == id,
 338:       );
 339:       return (item as dynamic).name as String;
 340:     } catch (_) {
 341:       return fallback;
 342:     }
 343:   }
 344:   Widget _infoRow(
 345:     BuildContext context,
 346:     IconData icon,
 347:     String text,
 348:   ) {
 349:     return Row(
 350:       children: [
 351:         Icon(icon, size: 16, color: AppColors.grey500),
 352:         const SizedBox(width: 8),
 353:         Expanded(
 354:           child: Text(
 355:             text,
 356:             style: Theme.of(context).textTheme.bodyMedium,
 357:           ),
 358:         ),
 359:       ],
 360:     );
 361:   }
 362:   (String, Color) _statusInfo(String status) {
 363:     return switch (status) {
 364:       'confirmed' => ('Confirmado', AppColors.success),
 365:       'completed' => ('Concluido', AppColors.info),
 366:       'canceled' => ('Cancelado', AppColors.error),
 367:       _ => ('Pendente', AppColors.warning),
 368:     };
 369:   }
 370: }

   7: class ProfileScreen extends ConsumerStatefulWidget {
   8:   const ProfileScreen({super.key});
   9:   @override
  10:   ConsumerState<ProfileScreen> createState() => _ProfileScreenState();
  11: }
  12: class _ProfileScreenState extends ConsumerState<ProfileScreen> {
  13:   final _formKey = GlobalKey<FormState>();
  14:   final _nameCtrl = TextEditingController();
  15:   final _emailCtrl = TextEditingController();
  16:   final _phoneCtrl = TextEditingController();
  17:   final _whatsappCtrl = TextEditingController();
  18:   final _addressCtrl = TextEditingController();
  19:   final _currentPassCtrl = TextEditingController();
  20:   final _newPassCtrl = TextEditingController();
  21:   final _confirmPassCtrl = TextEditingController();
  22:   bool _loading = false;
  23:   bool _showChangePassword = false;
  24:   bool _obscureCurrent = true;
  25:   bool _obscureNew = true;
  26:   bool _obscureConfirm = true;
  27:   bool _whatsappSameAsPhone = false;
  28:   bool _initialized = false;
  29:   @override
  30:   void dispose() {
  31:     _nameCtrl.dispose();
  32:     _emailCtrl.dispose();
  33:     _phoneCtrl.dispose();
  34:     _whatsappCtrl.dispose();
  35:     _addressCtrl.dispose();
  36:     _currentPassCtrl.dispose();
  37:     _newPassCtrl.dispose();
  38:     _confirmPassCtrl.dispose();
  39:     super.dispose();
  40:   }
  41:   void _initFields(String name, String email, String phone, String whatsapp, String address) {
  42:     if (!_initialized) {
  43:       _nameCtrl.text = name;
  44:       _emailCtrl.text = email;
  45:       _phoneCtrl.text = phone;
  46:       _whatsappCtrl.text = whatsapp;
  47:       _addressCtrl.text = address;
  48:       // Se telefone e whatsapp são iguais e não vazios, marca o checkbox
  49:       if (phone.isNotEmpty && phone == whatsapp) {
  50:         _whatsappSameAsPhone = true;
  51:       }
  52:       _initialized = true;
  53:     }
  54:   }
  55:   /// Remove tudo que não for dígito
  56:   String _onlyDigits(String v) => v.replaceAll(RegExp(r'\D'), '');
  57:   void _onPhoneChanged(String value) {
  58:     if (_whatsappSameAsPhone) {
  59:       _whatsappCtrl.text = value;
  60:     }
  61:   }
  62:   void _onWhatsappSameToggled(bool? checked) {
  63:     setState(() {
  64:       _whatsappSameAsPhone = checked ?? false;
  65:       if (_whatsappSameAsPhone) {
  66:         _whatsappCtrl.text = _phoneCtrl.text;
  67:       }
  68:     });
  69:   }
  70:   Future<void> _save() async {
  71:     if (!_formKey.currentState!.validate()) return;
  72:     final user = FirebaseAuth.instance.currentUser;
  73:     if (user == null) return;
  74:     setState(() => _loading = true);
  75:     try {
  76:       final newName = _nameCtrl.text.trim();
  77:       final newEmail = _emailCtrl.text.trim();
  78:       final newPhone = _onlyDigits(_phoneCtrl.text);
  79:       final newWhatsapp = _whatsappSameAsPhone
  80:           ? newPhone
  81:           : _onlyDigits(_whatsappCtrl.text);
  82:       final newAddress = _addressCtrl.text.trim();
  83:       // Atualiza email no Auth se mudou
  84:       if (newEmail != user.email) {
  85:         await user.verifyBeforeUpdateEmail(newEmail);
  86:         if (mounted) {
  87:           ScaffoldMessenger.of(context).showSnackBar(
  88:             const SnackBar(
  89:               content: Text(
  90:                 'Um link de verificacao foi enviado para o novo e-mail. '
  91:                 'O e-mail so sera atualizado apos confirmacao.',
  92:               ),
  93:               duration: Duration(seconds: 5),
  94:             ),
  95:           );
  96:         }
  97:       }
  98:       // Atualiza dados no Firestore
  99:       await FirebaseFirestore.instance
 100:           .collection('users')
 101:           .doc(user.uid)
 102:           .update({
 103:         'name': newName,
 104:         'phone': newPhone,
 105:         'whatsapp': newWhatsapp,
 106:         'address': newAddress,
 107:       });
 108:       // Atualiza senha se solicitado
 109:       if (_showChangePassword && _newPassCtrl.text.isNotEmpty) {
 110:         final credential = EmailAuthProvider.credential(
 111:           email: user.email!,
 112:           password: _currentPassCtrl.text,
 113:         );
 114:         await user.reauthenticateWithCredential(credential);
 115:         await user.updatePassword(_newPassCtrl.text);
 116:         _currentPassCtrl.clear();
 117:         _newPassCtrl.clear();
 118:         _confirmPassCtrl.clear();
 119:         setState(() => _showChangePassword = false);
 120:       }
 121:       if (mounted) {
 122:         ScaffoldMessenger.of(context).showSnackBar(
 123:           const SnackBar(content: Text('Perfil atualizado com sucesso.')),
 124:         );
 125:       }
 126:     } on FirebaseAuthException catch (e) {
 127:       if (!mounted) return;
 128:       final msg = switch (e.code) {
 129:         'wrong-password' => 'Senha atual incorreta.',
 130:         'requires-recent-login' =>
 131:           'Sessao expirada. Saia e entre novamente para alterar dados sensiveis.',
 132:         'email-already-in-use' => 'Este e-mail ja esta em uso.',
 133:         _ => e.message ?? 'Erro ao atualizar perfil.',
 134:       };
 135:       ScaffoldMessenger.of(context)
 136:           .showSnackBar(SnackBar(content: Text(msg)));
 137:     } catch (e) {
 138:       if (mounted) {
 139:         ScaffoldMessenger.of(context)
 140:             .showSnackBar(SnackBar(content: Text('Erro: $e')));
 141:       }
 142:     } finally {
 143:       if (mounted) setState(() => _loading = false);
 144:     }
 145:   }
 146:   @override
 147:   Widget build(BuildContext context) {
 148:     final userAsync = ref.watch(userRoleProvider);

 128:   void _agendar(BuildContext context, WidgetRef ref) {
 129:     // Pré-seleciona o serviço e reseta o restante do fluxo
 130:     ref.read(selectedServiceProvider.notifier).state = service;
 131:     ref.read(selectedBranchProvider.notifier).state = null;
 132:     ref.read(selectedDateProvider.notifier).state = null;
 133:     ref.read(selectedSlotProvider.notifier).state = null;
 134:     ref.read(selectedConsultantProvider.notifier).state = null;
 135:     ref.read(consultantHasConflictProvider.notifier).state = false;
 136: 
 137:     Navigator.of(context).push(
 138:       MaterialPageRoute(
 139:         builder: (_) => const VehicleSelectionScreen(isFromBooking: true),
 140:       ),
 141:     );
 142:   }
 143: 
 144:   String _formatDuration(int minutes) {
 145:     if (minutes < 60) return '${minutes}min';
 146:     final h = minutes ~/ 60;
 147:     final m = minutes % 60;
 148:     return m == 0 ? '${h}h' : '${h}h ${m}min';
 149:   }
 150: }

   1: import 'package:flutter/material.dart';
   2: import 'package:flutter_riverpod/flutter_riverpod.dart';
   3: import 'package:lavamax/core/constants/app_dimensions.dart';
   4: import 'package:lavamax/core/constants/app_strings.dart';
   5: import 'package:lavamax/presentation/providers/service_provider.dart';
   6: import 'package:lavamax/presentation/screens/slot_selection_screen.dart';
   7: import 'package:lavamax/presentation/widgets/custom_app_bar.dart';
   8: import 'package:lavamax/presentation/widgets/service_card.dart';
   9: class ServiceSelectionScreen extends ConsumerWidget {
  10:   const ServiceSelectionScreen({super.key});
  11:   @override
  12:   Widget build(BuildContext context, WidgetRef ref) {
  13:     final servicesAsync = ref.watch(servicesProvider);
  14:     return Scaffold(
  15:       appBar: CustomAppBar(
  16:         title: AppStrings.selectService,
  17:         showBackButton: true,
  18:       ),
  19:       body: servicesAsync.when(
  20:         data: (services) {
  21:           if (services.isEmpty) {
  22:             return Center(child: Text(AppStrings.noServicesAvailable));
  23:           }
  24:           // Ordena por sort_order; empate desempata por nome
  25:           final sorted = [...services]
  26:             ..sort((a, b) {
  27:               final byOrder = a.sortOrder.compareTo(b.sortOrder);
  28:               if (byOrder != 0) return byOrder;
  29:               return a.name.toLowerCase().compareTo(b.name.toLowerCase());
  30:             });
  31:           return ListView.builder(
  32:             padding:
  33:                 const EdgeInsets.all(AppDimensions.screenPaddingHorizontal),
  34:             itemCount: sorted.length,
  35:             itemBuilder: (context, index) {
  36:               final service = sorted[index];
  37:               return Padding(
  38:                 padding: const EdgeInsets.only(
  39:                     bottom: AppDimensions.paddingMedium),
  40:                 child: ServiceCard(
  41:                   service: service,
  42:                   onTap: () {
  43:                     ref.read(selectedServiceProvider.notifier).state =
  44:                         service;
  45:                     Navigator.of(context).push(
  46:                       MaterialPageRoute(
  47:                         builder: (_) => const SlotSelectionScreen(),
  48:                       ),
  49:                     );
  50:                   },
  51:                 ),
  52:               );
  53:             },
  54:           );
  55:         },
  56:         loading: () =>
  57:             const Center(child: CircularProgressIndicator()),
  58:         error: (error, stack) =>
  59:             Center(child: Text('Erro: $error')),
  60:       ),
  61:     );
  62:   }
  63: }

  20:         foregroundColor: AppColors.white,

  28:           height: 36,
  29:           fit: BoxFit.contain,
  30:         ),

  32:       ),

  45:                 onPressed: () => ref.invalidate(servicesProvider),
  46:                 child: const Text('Tentar novamente'),
  47:               ),
  48:             ],
  49:           ),
  50:         ),
  51:         data: (services) {
  52:           if (services.isEmpty) {
  53:             return const Center(child: Text('Nenhum serviço disponível.'));
  54:           }
  55:           final sorted = [...services]
  56:             ..sort((a, b) {
  57:               final byOrder = a.sortOrder.compareTo(b.sortOrder);
  58:               if (byOrder != 0) return byOrder;
  59:               return a.name.toLowerCase().compareTo(b.name.toLowerCase());
  60:             });
  61:           return GridView.builder(
  62:             padding:
  63:                 const EdgeInsets.all(AppDimensions.screenPaddingHorizontal),

  67:               mainAxisSpacing: AppDimensions.paddingMedium,
  68:               childAspectRatio: 1.4,
  69:             ),
  70:             itemCount: sorted.length,
  71:             itemBuilder: (context, index) {
  72:               return _ServiceCard(service: sorted[index]);
  73:             },
  74:           );
  75:         },
  76:       ),
  77:     );
  78:   }
  79: }

   1: import 'package:flutter/material.dart';
   2: import 'package:flutter_riverpod/flutter_riverpod.dart';
   3: import 'package:intl/intl.dart';
   4: import 'package:lavamax/core/constants/app_dimensions.dart';
   5: import 'package:lavamax/core/constants/app_strings.dart';
   6: import 'package:lavamax/presentation/providers/branch_provider.dart';
   7: import 'package:lavamax/presentation/providers/slot_provider.dart';
   8: import 'package:lavamax/presentation/screens/appointment_confirmation_screen.dart';
   9: import 'package:lavamax/presentation/widgets/custom_app_bar.dart';
  10: import 'package:lavamax/presentation/widgets/slot_card.dart';
  11: class SlotSelectionScreen extends ConsumerStatefulWidget {
  12:   const SlotSelectionScreen({super.key});
  13:   @override
  14:   ConsumerState<SlotSelectionScreen> createState() =>
  15:       _SlotSelectionScreenState();
  16: }
  17: class _SlotSelectionScreenState extends ConsumerState<SlotSelectionScreen> {
  18:   late DateTime _selectedDate;
  19:   final _nextButtonKey = GlobalKey();
  20:   @override
  21:   void initState() {
  22:     super.initState();
  23:     _selectedDate = DateTime.now();
  24:   }
  25:   @override
  26:   Widget build(BuildContext context) {
  27:     final selectedBranch = ref.watch(selectedBranchProvider);
  28:     final selectedDate = ref.watch(selectedDateProvider);
  29:     final dateToUse = selectedDate ?? _selectedDate;
  30:     // ref.watch do slot selecionado fica AQUI, fora do itemBuilder,
  31:     // para evitar rebuild desnecessário de toda a grid a cada seleção.
  32:     final selectedSlot = ref.watch(selectedSlotProvider);
  33:     if (selectedBranch == null) {
  34:       return Scaffold(
  35:         appBar: CustomAppBar(title: AppStrings.selectDateTime),
  36:         body: const Center(child: Text('Erro: Filial não selecionada')),
  37:       );
  38:     }
  39:     final slotsAsync = ref.watch(
  40:       availableSlotsProvider((selectedBranch.id, dateToUse)),
  41:     );
  42:     return Scaffold(
  43:       appBar: CustomAppBar(
  44:         title: AppStrings.selectDateTime,
  45:         showBackButton: true,
  46:       ),
  47:       body: SingleChildScrollView(
  48:         child: Padding(
  49:           padding:
  50:               const EdgeInsets.all(AppDimensions.screenPaddingHorizontal),
  51:           child: Column(
  52:             crossAxisAlignment: CrossAxisAlignment.stretch,
  53:             children: [
  54:               const SizedBox(height: AppDimensions.paddingMedium),
  55:               Text(
  56:                 'Selecione a Data',
  57:                 style: Theme.of(context).textTheme.titleMedium?.copyWith(
  58:                       fontWeight: FontWeight.bold,
  59:                     ),
  60:               ),
  61:               const SizedBox(height: AppDimensions.paddingMedium),
  62:               ElevatedButton.icon(
  63:                 onPressed: () async {
  64:                   final pickedDate = await showDatePicker(
  65:                     context: context,
  66:                     initialDate: dateToUse,
  67:                     firstDate: DateTime.now(),
  68:                     lastDate:
  69:                         DateTime.now().add(const Duration(days: 60)),
  70:                   );
  71:                   if (pickedDate != null) {
  72:                     ref.read(selectedDateProvider.notifier).state =
  73:                         pickedDate;
  74:                     // Limpa o slot selecionado ao trocar de data
  75:                     ref.read(selectedSlotProvider.notifier).state = null;
  76:                   }
  77:                 },
  78:                 icon: const Icon(Icons.calendar_today),
  79:                 label: Text(DateFormat('dd/MM/yyyy').format(dateToUse)),
  80:               ),
  81:               const SizedBox(height: AppDimensions.paddingLarge),
  82:               Text(
  83:                 AppStrings.availableSlots,
  84:                 style: Theme.of(context).textTheme.titleMedium?.copyWith(
  85:                       fontWeight: FontWeight.bold,
  86:                     ),
  87:               ),
  88:               const SizedBox(height: AppDimensions.paddingMedium),
  89:               slotsAsync.when(
  90:                 data: (slots) {
  91:                   if (slots.isEmpty) {
  92:                     return Center(
  93:                       child: Text(AppStrings.noSlotsAvailable),
  94:                     );
  95:                   }
  96:                   return GridView.builder(
  97:                     shrinkWrap: true,
  98:                     physics: const NeverScrollableScrollPhysics(),
  99:                     gridDelegate:
 100:                         const SliverGridDelegateWithFixedCrossAxisCount(
 101:                       crossAxisCount: 3,
 102:                       crossAxisSpacing: AppDimensions.paddingSmall,
 103:                       mainAxisSpacing: AppDimensions.paddingSmall,
 104:                       childAspectRatio: 1.8,
 105:                     ),
 106:                     itemCount: slots.length,
 107:                     itemBuilder: (context, index) {
 108:                       final slot = slots[index];
 109:                       // selectedSlot já foi obtido acima — sem watch aqui
 110:                       final isSelected = selectedSlot?.id == slot.id;
 111:                       return SlotCard(
 112:                         slot: slot,
 113:                         isSelected: isSelected,
 114:                         onTap: () {
 115:                           ref
 116:                               .read(selectedSlotProvider.notifier)
 117:                               .state = slot;
 118:                           // Rola até o botão "Próximo" após selecionar
 119:                           WidgetsBinding.instance.addPostFrameCallback((_) {
 120:                             final ctx = _nextButtonKey.currentContext;
 121:                             if (ctx != null) {
 122:                               Scrollable.ensureVisible(
 123:                                 ctx,
 124:                                 duration:
 125:                                     const Duration(milliseconds: 400),
 126:                                 curve: Curves.easeOut,
 127:                                 alignment: 1.0,
 128:                               );
 129:                             }
 130:                           });
 131:                         },
 132:                       );
 133:                     },
 134:                   );
 135:                 },
 136:                 loading: () =>
 137:                     const Center(child: CircularProgressIndicator()),
 138:                 error: (error, stackTrace) =>
 139:                     Center(child: Text('Erro: $error')),
 140:               ),
 141:               const SizedBox(height: AppDimensions.paddingLarge),
 142:               ElevatedButton(
 143:                 key: _nextButtonKey,
 144:                 onPressed: () {
 145:                   if (selectedSlot != null) {
 146:                     Navigator.of(context).push(
 147:                       MaterialPageRoute(
 148:                         builder: (context) =>
 149:                             const AppointmentConfirmationScreen(),
 150:                       ),
 151:                     );
 152:                   } else {
 153:                     ScaffoldMessenger.of(context).showSnackBar(

 152:                                 AppDimensions.buttonHeight),
 153:                           ),

 160:             ],

 162:         },

 164:         error: (e, stack) => Center(child: Text('Erro: $e')),
 165:       ),
 166:     );
 167:   }
 168:   /// Reseta filial/serviço/slot/consultor e avança para seleção de filial.
 169:   void _advance(BuildContext context, WidgetRef ref) {
 170:     ref.read(selectedBranchProvider.notifier).state = null;
 171:     ref.read(selectedServiceProvider.notifier).state = null;
 172:     ref.read(selectedDateProvider.notifier).state = null;
 173:     ref.read(selectedSlotProvider.notifier).state = null;
 174:     ref.read(selectedConsultantProvider.notifier).state = null;
 175:     ref.read(consultantHasConflictProvider.notifier).state = false;
 176:     Navigator.of(context).push(
 177:       MaterialPageRoute(
 178:         builder: (_) => const BranchSelectionScreen(),
 179:       ),
 180:     );
 181:   }
 182:   Future<bool> _confirmDelete(
 183:       BuildContext context, VehicleModel vehicle) async {
 184:     return await showDialog<bool>(
 185:           context: context,
 186:           builder: (_) => AlertDialog(
 187:             title: const Text('Excluir veiculo'),
 188:             content: Text(
 189:               'Deseja excluir ${vehicle.brand} ${vehicle.model} (${formatPlate(vehicle.plate)})?',
 190:             ),
 191:             actions: [
 192:               TextButton(
 193:                 onPressed: () => Navigator.pop(context, false),
 194:                 child: const Text('Cancelar'),
 195:               ),
 196:               FilledButton(
 197:                 style: FilledButton.styleFrom(
 198:                     backgroundColor: AppColors.error),
 199:                 onPressed: () => Navigator.pop(context, true),
 200:                 child: const Text('Excluir'),
 201:               ),
 202:             ],
 203:           ),
 204:         ) ??
 205:         false;
 206:   }
 207:   void _deleteVehicle(
 208:       BuildContext context, WidgetRef ref, VehicleModel vehicle) {
 209:     final uid = FirebaseAuth.instance.currentUser?.uid;
 210:     if (uid == null) return;
 211:     ref
 212:         .read(vehicleRepositoryProvider)
 213:         .deleteVehicle(uid, vehicle.id);
 214:     ref.invalidate(userVehiclesProvider);
 215:     ScaffoldMessenger.of(context).showSnackBar(
 216:       SnackBar(
 217:           content:
 218:               Text('${vehicle.brand} ${vehicle.model} removido.')),
 219:     );
 220:   }
 221:   void _goToAddVehicle(BuildContext context, WidgetRef ref) {
 222:     Navigator.push(
 223:       context,
 224:       MaterialPageRoute(builder: (_) => const AddVehicleScreen()),
 225:     );
 226:   }
 227: }

  11: class AdminAppointmentsScreen extends StatefulWidget {
  12:   const AdminAppointmentsScreen({super.key});
  13:   @override
  14:   State<AdminAppointmentsScreen> createState() =>
  15:       _AdminAppointmentsScreenState();
  16: }
  17: class _AdminAppointmentsScreenState
  18:     extends State<AdminAppointmentsScreen> {
  19:   final _repo = AppointmentRepository(FirebaseService().firestore);
  20:   final _branchRepo = BranchRepository(FirebaseService().firestore);
  21:   final _serviceRepo = ServiceRepository(FirebaseService().firestore);
  22:   List<AppointmentModel> _all = [];
  23:   List<BranchModel> _branches = [];
  24:   List<ServiceModel> _services = [];
  25:   bool _loading = true;
  26:   String? _error;
  27:   String _statusFilter = 'all';
  28:   String? _branchFilter;
  29:   @override
  30:   void initState() {
  31:     super.initState();
  32:     _load();
  33:   }
  34:   Future<void> _load() async {
  35:     setState(() {
  36:       _loading = true;
  37:       _error = null;
  38:     });
  39:     try {
  40:       final results = await Future.wait([
  41:         _repo.getAllAppointments(),
  42:         _branchRepo.getAllBranches(),
  43:         _serviceRepo.getAllServices(),
  44:       ]);
  45:       if (mounted) {
  46:         setState(() {
  47:           _all = results[0] as List<AppointmentModel>;
  48:           _branches = results[1] as List<BranchModel>;
  49:           _services = results[2] as List<ServiceModel>;
  50:         });
  51:       }
  52:     } catch (e) {
  53:       if (mounted) setState(() => _error = e.toString());
  54:     } finally {
  55:       if (mounted) setState(() => _loading = false);
  56:     }
  57:   }
  58:   List<AppointmentModel> get _filtered {
  59:     return _all.where((a) {
  60:       final statusOk =
  61:           _statusFilter == 'all' || a.status == _statusFilter;
  62:       final branchOk =
  63:           _branchFilter == null || a.branchId == _branchFilter;
  64:       return statusOk && branchOk;
  65:     }).toList()
  66:       ..sort((a, b) =>
  67:           b.appointmentDate.compareTo(a.appointmentDate));
  68:   }
  69:   Future<void> _delete(AppointmentModel appointment) async {
  70:     final code = appointment.id.substring(0, 8).toUpperCase();
  71:     final confirm = await showDialog<bool>(
  72:       context: context,
  73:       builder: (_) => AlertDialog(
  74:         title: const Text('Excluir agendamento'),
  75:         content: Text(
  76:           'Excluir agendamento #$code?\n\n'
  77:           'Esta acao nao pode ser desfeita. '
  78:           'O slot sera liberado automaticamente se necessario.',
  79:         ),
  80:         actions: [
  81:           TextButton(
  82:             onPressed: () => Navigator.pop(context, false),
  83:             child: const Text('Cancelar'),
  84:           ),
  85:           FilledButton(
  86:             style:
  87:                 FilledButton.styleFrom(backgroundColor: AppColors.error),
  88:             onPressed: () => Navigator.pop(context, true),
  89:             child: const Text('Excluir'),
  90:           ),
  91:         ],
  92:       ),
  93:     );
  94:     if (confirm == true) {
  95:       try {
  96:         await _repo.deleteAppointment(appointment.id);
  97:         if (mounted) {
  98:           setState(
  99:               () => _all.removeWhere((a) => a.id == appointment.id));
 100:           ScaffoldMessenger.of(context).showSnackBar(
 101:             const SnackBar(content: Text('Agendamento excluido.')),
 102:           );
 103:         }
 104:       } catch (e) {
 105:         if (mounted) {
 106:           ScaffoldMessenger.of(context).showSnackBar(
 107:             SnackBar(content: Text('Erro ao excluir: $e')),
 108:           );
 109:         }
 110:       }
 111:     }
 112:   }
 113:   @override
 114:   Widget build(BuildContext context) {
 115:     final filtered = _filtered;
 116:     return Scaffold(
 117:       appBar: AppBar(
 118:         title: const Text('Agendamentos'),
 119:         actions: [
 120:           IconButton(
 121:             icon: const Icon(Icons.refresh),
 122:             tooltip: 'Atualizar',
 123:             onPressed: _load,
 124:           ),
 125:         ],
 126:       ),
 127:       body: _loading
 128:           ? const Center(child: CircularProgressIndicator())
 129:           : _error != null
 130:               ? Center(
 131:                   child: Column(
 132:                     mainAxisAlignment: MainAxisAlignment.center,
 133:                     children: [
 134:                       Text('Erro: $_error',
 135:                           style:
 136:                               const TextStyle(color: AppColors.error)),
 137:                       const SizedBox(height: 16),
 138:                       ElevatedButton(
 139:                           onPressed: _load,
 140:                           child: const Text('Tentar novamente')),
 141:                     ],
 142:                   ),
 143:                 )
 144:               : Column(
 145:                   children: [
 146:                     // Filtros
 147:                     _FilterBar(
 148:                       statusFilter: _statusFilter,
 149:                       branchFilter: _branchFilter,
 150:                       branches: _branches,
 151:                       onStatusChanged: (v) =>
 152:                           setState(() => _statusFilter = v),
 153:                       onBranchChanged: (v) =>
 154:                           setState(() => _branchFilter = v),
 155:                     ),
 156:                     // Contador
 157:                     Padding(
 158:                       padding: const EdgeInsets.symmetric(
 159:                           horizontal: 16, vertical: 6),
 160:                       child: Row(
 161:                         children: [
 162:                           Text(
 163:                             '${filtered.length} agendamento(s)',
 164:                             style: const TextStyle(
 165:                                 fontSize: 12, color: AppColors.grey500),
 166:                           ),
 167:                         ],
 168:                       ),
 169:                     ),
 170:                     Expanded(
 171:                       child: filtered.isEmpty
 172:                           ? const Center(
 173:                               child: Text(
 174:                                   'Nenhum agendamento encontrado.'))
 175:                           : ListView.separated(
 176:                               padding: const EdgeInsets.fromLTRB(
 177:                                   16, 0, 16, 16),
 178:                               itemCount: filtered.length,
 179:                               separatorBuilder: (_, _) =>
 180:                                   const SizedBox(height: 8),
 181:                               itemBuilder: (_, i) => _AppointmentRow(
 182:                                 appointment: filtered[i],
 183:                                 services: _services,
 184:                                 onDelete: () => _delete(filtered[i]),
 185:                               ),
 186:                             ),
 187:                     ),
 188:                   ],
 189:                 ),
 190:     );
 191:   }
 192: }

 194: // Barra de filtros
 195: // ─────────────────────────────────────────
 196: class _FilterBar extends StatelessWidget {
 197:   final String statusFilter;
 198:   final String? branchFilter;
 199:   final List<BranchModel> branches;
 200:   final void Function(String) onStatusChanged;
 201:   final void Function(String?) onBranchChanged;
 202:   const _FilterBar({
 203:     required this.statusFilter,
 204:     required this.branchFilter,
 205:     required this.branches,
 206:     required this.onStatusChanged,
 207:     required this.onBranchChanged,
 208:   });
 209:   @override
 210:   Widget build(BuildContext context) {
 211:     final statuses = [
 212:       ('all', 'Todos'),
 213:       ('pending', 'Pendente'),
 214:       ('confirmed', 'Confirmado'),
 215:       ('completed', 'Concluido'),
 216:       ('canceled', 'Cancelado'),
 217:     ];
 218:     return Container(
 219:       color: Theme.of(context).colorScheme.surfaceContainerHighest,
 220:       padding: const EdgeInsets.fromLTRB(12, 8, 12, 8),
 221:       child: Column(
 222:         crossAxisAlignment: CrossAxisAlignment.start,
 223:         children: [
 224:           // Chips de status
 225:           SingleChildScrollView(
 226:             scrollDirection: Axis.horizontal,
 227:             child: Row(
 228:               children: statuses
 229:                   .map(
 230:                     (s) => Padding(
 231:                       padding: const EdgeInsets.only(right: 6),
 232:                       child: FilterChip(
 233:                         label: Text(s.$2),
 234:                         selected: statusFilter == s.$1,
 235:                         onSelected: (_) => onStatusChanged(s.$1),
 236:                         visualDensity: VisualDensity.compact,
 237:                       ),
 238:                     ),
 239:                   )
 240:                   .toList(),
 241:             ),
 242:           ),
 243:           // Dropdown de filial
 244:           if (branches.isNotEmpty) ...[
 245:             const SizedBox(height: 6),
 246:             DropdownButtonFormField<String?>(
 247:               initialValue: branchFilter,
 248:               isDense: true,
 249:               decoration: const InputDecoration(
 250:                 labelText: 'Filial',
 251:                 border: OutlineInputBorder(),
 252:                 contentPadding:
 253:                     EdgeInsets.symmetric(horizontal: 12, vertical: 8),
 254:               ),
 255:               items: [
 256:                 const DropdownMenuItem(
 257:                     value: null, child: Text('Todas as filiais')),
 258:                 ...branches.map(
 259:                   (b) => DropdownMenuItem(
 260:                       value: b.id, child: Text(b.name)),
 261:                 ),
 262:               ],
 263:               onChanged: onBranchChanged,
 264:             ),
 265:           ],
 266:         ],
 267:       ),
 268:     );
 269:   }
 270: }
 271: // ─────────────────────────────────────────
 272: // Row de agendamento
 273: // ─────────────────────────────────────────
 274: class _AppointmentRow extends StatelessWidget {
 275:   const _AppointmentRow({
 276:     required this.appointment,
 277:     required this.services,
 278:     required this.onDelete,
 279:   });
 280:   final AppointmentModel appointment;
 281:   final List<ServiceModel> services;
 282:   final VoidCallback onDelete;
 283:   @override
 284:   Widget build(BuildContext context) {
 285:     final dateFormat = DateFormat('dd/MM/yyyy HH:mm');
 286:     final statusInfo = _statusInfo(appointment.status);
 287:     // Preço: busca no ServiceModel; fallback para "—"
 288:     final service = services.cast<ServiceModel?>().firstWhere(
 289:           (s) => s?.id == appointment.serviceId,
 290:           orElse: () => null,
 291:         );
 292:     final priceLabel = service != null
 293:         ? NumberFormat.currency(locale: 'pt_BR', symbol: 'R\$')
 294:             .format(service.price)
 295:         : '—';
 296:     return Card(
 297:       child: ListTile(
 298:         leading: Container(
 299:           width: 4,
 300:           height: 40,
 301:           decoration: BoxDecoration(
 302:             color: statusInfo.$2,
 303:             borderRadius: BorderRadius.circular(2),
 304:           ),
 305:         ),
 306:         title: Text(
 307:           '${appointment.serviceName.isNotEmpty ? appointment.serviceName : 'Servico'} — ${appointment.branchName.isNotEmpty ? appointment.branchName : 'Filial'}',
 308:           style: const TextStyle(
 309:               fontWeight: FontWeight.bold, fontSize: 13),
 310:         ),
 311:         subtitle: Column(
 312:           crossAxisAlignment: CrossAxisAlignment.start,
 313:           children: [
 314:             Text(dateFormat.format(appointment.appointmentDate)),
 315:             if (appointment.consultantName.isNotEmpty)
 316:               Text(
 317:                 'Consultor: ${appointment.consultantName}',
 318:                 style: const TextStyle(
 319:                     fontSize: 12, color: AppColors.grey600),
 320:               ),
 321:             Text(
 322:               priceLabel,
 323:               style: const TextStyle(
 324:                   fontSize: 12,
 325:                   color: AppColors.grey700,
 326:                   fontWeight: FontWeight.w600),
 327:             ),
 328:           ],
 329:         ),
 330:         isThreeLine: true,
 331:         trailing: Row(
 332:           mainAxisSize: MainAxisSize.min,
 333:           children: [
 334:             Container(
 335:               padding:
 336:                   const EdgeInsets.symmetric(horizontal: 8, vertical: 3),
 337:               decoration: BoxDecoration(
 338:                 color: statusInfo.$2.withValues(alpha: 0.15),
 339:                 borderRadius: BorderRadius.circular(12),
 340:               ),
 341:               child: Text(
 342:                 statusInfo.$1,
 343:                 style: TextStyle(
 344:                   color: statusInfo.$2,
 345:                   fontSize: 11,
 346:                   fontWeight: FontWeight.bold,
 347:                 ),
 348:               ),
 349:             ),
 350:             IconButton(
 351:               icon: const Icon(Icons.delete_outline,
 352:                   color: AppColors.error, size: 20),
 353:               onPressed: onDelete,
 354:             ),
 355:           ],
 356:         ),
 357:       ),
 358:     );
 359:   }
 360:   (String, Color) _statusInfo(String status) {
 361:     return switch (status) {
 362:       'confirmed' => ('Confirmado', AppColors.success),
 363:       'completed' => ('Concluido', AppColors.info),
 364:       'canceled' => ('Cancelado', AppColors.error),
 365:       _ => ('Pendente', AppColors.warning),
 366:     };
 367:   }
 368: }
