  21:       context: context,
  22:       builder: (_) => AlertDialog(
  23:         title: Text(id == null ? 'Nova Filial' : 'Editar Filial'),
  24:         content: Column(
  25:           mainAxisSize: MainAxisSize.min,
  26:           children: [
  27:             TextField(
  28:               controller: nameCtrl,
  29:               textCapitalization: TextCapitalization.words,
  30:               decoration: const InputDecoration(labelText: 'Nome'),
  31:             ),
  32:             const SizedBox(height: 12),
  33:             TextField(
  34:               controller: addressCtrl,
  35:               textCapitalization: TextCapitalization.words,
  36:               decoration: const InputDecoration(labelText: 'Endereco'),
  37:             ),
  38:           ],
  39:         ),
  40:         actions: [
  41:           TextButton(
  42:             onPressed: () => Navigator.pop(context),
  43:             child: const Text('Cancelar'),
  44:           ),
  45:           FilledButton(
  46:             onPressed: () async {
  47:               final name = nameCtrl.text.trim();
  48:               final address = addressCtrl.text.trim();
  49:               if (name.isEmpty) return;
  50:               // UX 3: inclui timestamps em criação e edição
  51:               if (id == null) {
  52:                 await _db.collection('branches').add({
  53:                   'name': name,
  54:                   'address': address,
  55:                   'is_active': true,
  56:                   'created_at': FieldValue.serverTimestamp(),
  57:                   'updated_at': FieldValue.serverTimestamp(),
  58:                 });
  59:               } else {
  60:                 await _db.collection('branches').doc(id).update({
  61:                   'name': name,
  62:                   'address': address,
  63:                   'is_active': data?['is_active'] ?? true,
  64:                   'updated_at': FieldValue.serverTimestamp(),
  65:                 });
  66:               }
  67:               if (mounted) Navigator.pop(context);
  68:             },
  69:             child: const Text('Salvar'),
  70:           ),
  71:         ],
  72:       ),
  73:     );
  74:   }
  75:   Future<void> _toggleActive(String id, bool current) async {
  76:     await _db
  77:         .collection('branches')
  78:         .doc(id)
  79:         .update({
  80:       'is_active': !current,
  81:       'updated_at': FieldValue.serverTimestamp(),
  82:     });
  83:   }
  84:   Future<void> _delete(String id, String name) async {
  85:     // Seg 3: verifica agendamentos ativos antes de excluir
  86:     final activeSnap = await _db
  87:         .collection('appointments')
  88:         .where('branch_id', isEqualTo: id)
  89:         .where('status', whereIn: ['pending', 'confirmed'])
  90:         .limit(1)
  91:         .get();
  92:     if (activeSnap.docs.isNotEmpty) {
  93:       if (!mounted) return;
  94:       if (true) {
  95:         showDialog(
  96:           context: context,
  97:           builder: (_) => AlertDialog(
  98:             title: const Text('Exclusao bloqueada'),
  99:             content: Text(
 100:               'A filial "$name" possui agendamentos ativos.\n\n'
 101:               'Cancele ou conclua todos os agendamentos antes de excluir.',
 102:             ),
 103:             actions: [
 104:               FilledButton(
 105:                 onPressed: () => Navigator.pop(context),
 106:                 child: const Text('Entendi'),
 107:               ),
 108:             ],
 109:           ),
 110:         );
 111:       }
 112:       return;
 113:     }
 114:     if (!mounted) return;
 115:     final confirm = await showDialog<bool>(
 116:       context: context,
 117:       builder: (_) => AlertDialog(
 118:         title: const Text('Excluir filial'),
 119:         content: Text('Deseja excluir "$name"?'),
 120:         actions: [
 121:           TextButton(
 122:             onPressed: () => Navigator.pop(context, false),
 123:             child: const Text('Cancelar'),
 124:           ),
 125:           FilledButton(
 126:             style: FilledButton.styleFrom(backgroundColor: Colors.red),
 127:             onPressed: () => Navigator.pop(context, true),
 128:             child: const Text('Excluir'),
 129:           ),
 130:         ],
 131:       ),
 132:     );
 133:     if (confirm == true) {
 134:       await _db.collection('branches').doc(id).delete();
 135:     }
 136:   }

 143:         child: const Icon(Icons.add),
 144:       ),
 145:       body: StreamBuilder<QuerySnapshot>(
 146:         stream: _db.collection('branches').orderBy('name').snapshots(),
 147:         builder: (_, snap) {
 148:           if (snap.connectionState == ConnectionState.waiting) {
 149:             return const Center(child: CircularProgressIndicator());
 150:           }
 151:           final docs = snap.data?.docs ?? [];
 152:           return ListView.builder(
 153:             itemCount: docs.length,
 154:             itemBuilder: (_, i) {

 156:               final d = doc.data() as Map<String, dynamic>;
 157:               final name = d['name'] as String? ?? '';
 158:               final address = d['address'] as String? ?? '';
 159:               final isActive = d['is_active'] as bool? ?? true;
 160:               return ListTile(

 163:                   color: isActive ? Colors.green : Colors.grey,
 164:                 ),

 171:   Widget _buildBrandList() {
 172:     return StreamBuilder<QuerySnapshot>(
 173:       stream: _db
 174:           .collection('vehicle_brands')
 175:           .orderBy('name')
 176:           .snapshots(),
 177:       builder: (_, snap) {

 215:     );

 224:         final data = snap.data?.data() as Map<String, dynamic>?;

 227:         // UX 5: _currentModels atualizado dentro de setState
 228:         WidgetsBinding.instance.addPostFrameCallback((_) {

 115: // ── Formatter de telefone: (XX)XXXXX-XXXX ──────────────────────
 116: class _PhoneFormatter extends TextInputFormatter {
 117:   @override
 118:   TextEditingValue formatEditUpdate(
 119:       TextEditingValue oldValue, TextEditingValue newValue) {
 120:     final digits = newValue.text.replaceAll(RegExp(r'[^0-9]'), '');
 121:     if (digits.isEmpty) return newValue.copyWith(text: '');
 122:     final d = digits.length > 11 ? digits.substring(0, 11) : digits;
 123:     String formatted;
 124:     if (d.length <= 2) {
 125:       formatted = '($d';
 126:     } else if (d.length <= 7) {
 127:       formatted = '(${d.substring(0, 2)})${d.substring(2)}';
 128:     } else {
 129:       formatted =
 130:           '(${d.substring(0, 2)})${d.substring(2, 7)}-${d.substring(7)}';
 131:     }
 132:     return newValue.copyWith(
 133:       text: formatted,
 134:       selection: TextSelection.collapsed(offset: formatted.length),
 135:     );
 136:   }
 137: }
 138: class _ConsultantFormScreen extends StatefulWidget {
 139:   final ConsultantModel? consultant;
 140:   final ConsultantRepository repo;
 141:   final FirebaseFirestore db;
 142:   const _ConsultantFormScreen({
 143:     required this.consultant,
 144:     required this.repo,
 145:     required this.db,
 146:   });
 147:   @override
 148:   State<_ConsultantFormScreen> createState() => _ConsultantFormScreenState();
 149: }
 150: class _ConsultantFormScreenState extends State<_ConsultantFormScreen> {
 151:   final _formKey = GlobalKey<FormState>();
 152:   late final TextEditingController _nameCtrl;
 153:   late final TextEditingController _phoneCtrl;
 154:   late final TextEditingController _limitCtrl;
 155:   String? _selectedBranchId;
 156:   List<QueryDocumentSnapshot> _branchDocs = [];
 157:   bool _branchesLoading = true;
 158:   bool _saving = false;
 159:   @override
 160:   void initState() {
 161:     super.initState();
 162:     _nameCtrl = TextEditingController(text: widget.consultant?.name ?? '');
 163:     _phoneCtrl = TextEditingController(text: widget.consultant?.phone ?? '');
 164:     _limitCtrl = TextEditingController(
 165:       text: (widget.consultant?.dailyLimit ?? 16).toString(),
 166:     );
 167:     _selectedBranchId = widget.consultant?.branchId;
 168:     _loadBranches();
 169:   }
 170:   Future<void> _loadBranches() async {
 171:     try {
 172:       final snap = await widget.db
 173:           .collection('branches')
 174:           .where('is_active', isEqualTo: true)
 175:           .get();
 176:       if (mounted) {
 177:         final sorted = snap.docs.toList()
 178:           ..sort((a, b) =>
 179:               (a['name'] as String).compareTo(b['name'] as String));
 180:         setState(() => _branchDocs = sorted);
 181:       }
 182:     } catch (e) {
 183:       if (mounted) {
 184:         ScaffoldMessenger.of(context).showSnackBar(
 185:           SnackBar(content: Text('Erro ao carregar filiais: $e')),
 186:         );
 187:       }
 188:     } finally {
 189:       if (mounted) setState(() => _branchesLoading = false);
 190:     }
 191:   }
 192:   @override
 193:   void dispose() {
 194:     _nameCtrl.dispose();
 195:     _phoneCtrl.dispose();
 196:     _limitCtrl.dispose();
 197:     super.dispose();
 198:   }
 199:   Future<void> _save() async {
 200:     if (!_formKey.currentState!.validate()) return;
 201:     if (_selectedBranchId == null) {
 202:       ScaffoldMessenger.of(context).showSnackBar(
 203:         const SnackBar(content: Text('Selecione a filial')),
 204:       );
 205:       return;
 206:     }
 207:     final nav = Navigator.of(context);
 208:     setState(() => _saving = true);
 209:     try {
 210:       final name = _nameCtrl.text.trim();
 211:       final phone = _phoneCtrl.text.trim();
 212:       final limit = int.tryParse(_limitCtrl.text.trim()) ?? 16;
 213:       if (widget.consultant == null) {
 214:         await widget.repo.create(
 215:           ConsultantModel(
 216:             id: '',
 217:             name: name,
 218:             phone: phone,
 219:             branchId: _selectedBranchId!,
 220:             dailyLimit: limit,
 221:             isActive: true,
 222:           ),
 223:         );
 224:       } else {
 225:         await widget.repo.update(widget.consultant!.id, {
 226:           'name': name,
 227:           'phone': phone,
 228:           'branch_id': _selectedBranchId,
 229:           'daily_limit': limit,
 230:         });
 231:       }
 232:       nav.pop();
 233:     } catch (e) {
 234:       if (mounted) {
 235:         ScaffoldMessenger.of(context).showSnackBar(
 236:           SnackBar(content: Text('Erro ao salvar: $e')),
 237:         );
 238:       }
 239:     } finally {
 240:       if (mounted) setState(() => _saving = false);
 241:     }
 242:   }
 243:   @override
 244:   Widget build(BuildContext context) {
 245:     final isNew = widget.consultant == null;
 246:     return Scaffold(
 247:       appBar: AppBar(
 248:         title: Text(isNew ? 'Novo Consultor' : 'Editar Consultor'),
 249:       ),
 250:       body: _branchesLoading
 251:           ? const Center(child: CircularProgressIndicator())
 252:           : SingleChildScrollView(
 253:               padding: const EdgeInsets.all(24),
 254:               child: Form(
 255:                 key: _formKey,
 256:                 child: Column(
 257:                   crossAxisAlignment: CrossAxisAlignment.stretch,
 258:                   children: [
 259:                     TextFormField(
 260:                       controller: _nameCtrl,
 261:                       textCapitalization: TextCapitalization.words,
 262:                       decoration: const InputDecoration(
 263:                         labelText: 'Nome',
 264:                         prefixIcon: Icon(Icons.person_outline),
 265:                       ),
 266:                       validator: (v) => (v == null || v.trim().isEmpty)
 267:                           ? 'Informe o nome'
 268:                           : null,
 269:                     ),
 270:                     const SizedBox(height: 16),
 271:                     TextFormField(
 272:                       controller: _phoneCtrl,
 273:                       keyboardType: TextInputType.phone,
 274:                       inputFormatters: [_PhoneFormatter()],
 275:                       decoration: const InputDecoration(
 276:                         labelText: 'Telefone de contato',
 277:                         prefixIcon: Icon(Icons.phone_outlined),
 278:                         hintText: '(71)99999-9999',
 279:                       ),
 280:                     ),
 281:                     const SizedBox(height: 16),
 282:                     TextFormField(
 283:                       controller: _limitCtrl,
 284:                       keyboardType: TextInputType.number,
 285:                       decoration: const InputDecoration(
 286:                         labelText: 'Limite de atendimentos por dia',
 287:                         prefixIcon: Icon(Icons.event_available_outlined),
 288:                       ),
 289:                       validator: (v) => (int.tryParse(v ?? '') == null)
 290:                           ? 'Informe um numero valido'
 291:                           : null,
 292:                     ),
 293:                     const SizedBox(height: 16),
 294:                     DropdownButtonFormField<String>(
 295:                       decoration: const InputDecoration(
 296:                         labelText: 'Filial',
 297:                         prefixIcon: Icon(Icons.store_outlined),
 298:                       ),
 299:                       initialValue: _selectedBranchId,
 300:                       items: _branchDocs
 301:                           .map((d) => DropdownMenuItem<String>(
 302:                                 value: d.id,
 303:                                 child: Text(d['name'] as String),
 304:                               ))
 305:                           .toList(),
 306:                       onChanged: (v) =>
 307:                           setState(() => _selectedBranchId = v),
 308:                       validator: (v) =>
 309:                           v == null ? 'Selecione a filial' : null,
 310:                     ),

 321:                               ),
 322:                             )
 323:                           : const Text('Salvar'),
 324:                     ),
 325:                   ],
 326:                 ),
 327:               ),
 328:             ),
 329:     );

  84:   Future<void> _toggleCredit(CreditModel credit) async {
  85:     final isActive = credit.status == 'active';
  86:     final action = isActive ? 'cancelar' : 'reativar';
  87:     final confirm = await showDialog<bool>(
  88:       context: context,
  89:       builder: (_) => AlertDialog(
  90:         title: Text('${isActive ? 'Cancelar' : 'Reativar'} credito'),

 129:                     hintText: 'https://...',
 130:                   ),
 131:                   onChanged: (v) {
 132:                     if (v.isNotEmpty && pickedFile != null) {
 133:                       setInner(() => pickedFile = null);
 134:                     }
 135:                   },
 136:                 ),
 137:                 if (uploadError != null) ...[
 138:                   const SizedBox(height: 8),
 139:                   Text(
 140:                     uploadError!,
 141:                     style: const TextStyle(color: Colors.red, fontSize: 12),
 142:                   ),
 143:                 ],
 144:                 const SizedBox(height: 16),
 145:                 // ── Preço ──
 146:                 TextField(
 147:                   controller: priceCtrl,
 148:                   keyboardType: TextInputType.number,
 149:                   inputFormatters: [_BrlCurrencyFormatter()],
 150:                   decoration: const InputDecoration(
 151:                     labelText: 'Preço (R\$)',
 152:                     prefixText: 'R\$ ',
 153:                   ),
 154:                 ),
 155:                 const SizedBox(height: 12),
 156:                 // ── Duração ──
 157:                 TextField(
 158:                   controller: durationCtrl,
 159:                   keyboardType: TextInputType.number,
 160:                   decoration:
 161:                       const InputDecoration(labelText: 'Duração (minutos)'),
 162:                 ),
 163:               ],
 164:             ),
 165:           ),
 166:         ),
 167:         actions: [
 168:           TextButton(
 169:             onPressed: uploading ? null : () => Navigator.pop(ctx),
 170:             child: const Text('Cancelar'),
 171:           ),
 172:           StatefulBuilder(
 173:             builder: (context, setSave) => FilledButton(
 174:               onPressed: uploading
 175:                   ? null
 176:                   : () async {
 177:                       final name = nameCtrl.text.trim();
 178:                       if (name.isEmpty) return;
 179:                       setSave(() => uploading = true);
 180:                       try {
 181:                         String finalUrl = urlCtrl.text.trim();
 182:                         if (pickedFile != null) {
 183:                           final ext = pickedFile!.name.split('.').last;
 184:                           final storagePath =
 185:                               'services/icons/${_uuid.v4()}.$ext';
 186:                           final ref = _storage.ref(storagePath);
 187:                           await ref.putFile(
 188:                             File(pickedFile!.path),
 189:                             SettableMetadata(
 190:                               contentType: 'image/$ext',
 191:                               customMetadata: {
 192:                                 'cacheControl': 'public, max-age=31536000',
 193:                               },
 194:                             ),
 195:                           );
 196:                           finalUrl = await ref.getDownloadURL();
 197:                         }
 198:                         final payload = <String, dynamic>{
 199:                           'name': name,
 200:                           'description': descCtrl.text.trim(),
 201:                           'icon_url': finalUrl,
 202:                           'price': _parseBrl(priceCtrl.text),
 203:                           'duration_minutes':
 204:                               int.tryParse(durationCtrl.text.trim()) ?? 0,
 205:                           'sort_order':
 206:                               int.tryParse(sortOrderCtrl.text.trim()) ?? 0,
 207:                           'updated_at': FieldValue.serverTimestamp(),
 208:                         };
 209:                         if (id == null) {
 210:                           payload['is_active'] = true;
 211:                           payload['created_at'] =
 212:                               FieldValue.serverTimestamp();
 213:                           await _db.collection('services').add(payload);
 214:                         } else {
 215:                           payload['is_active'] = data?['is_active'] ?? true;
 216:                           await _db
 217:                               .collection('services')
 218:                               .doc(id)
 219:                               .update(payload);
 220:                         }
 221:                         if (ctx.mounted) Navigator.pop(ctx);
 222:                       } catch (e) {
 223:                         setSave(() {
 224:                           uploading = false;
 225:                           uploadError = 'Erro ao salvar: $e';
 226:                         });
 227:                         if (ctx.mounted) {
 228:                           ScaffoldMessenger.of(ctx).showSnackBar(
 229:                             SnackBar(content: Text('Erro ao salvar: $e')),
 230:                           );
 231:                         }
 232:                       }
 233:                     },
 234:               child: uploading
 235:                   ? const SizedBox(
 236:                       width: 18,
 237:                       height: 18,
 238:                       child: CircularProgressIndicator(
 239:                         strokeWidth: 2,
 240:                         color: Colors.white,
 241:                       ),
 242:                     )
 243:                   : const Text('Salvar'),
 244:             ),
 245:           ),
 246:         ],
 247:       ),
 248:     );
 249:   }
 250:   // ── Toggle ativo/inativo ───────────────────────────────────────────────────
 251:   Future<void> _toggleActive(String id, bool current) async {
 252:     await _db.collection('services').doc(id).update({
 253:       'is_active': !current,
 254:       'updated_at': FieldValue.serverTimestamp(),
 255:     });
 256:   }
 257:   // ── Exclusão ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
 258:   Future<void> _delete(String id, String name) async {
 259:     final activeSnap = await _db
 260:         .collection('appointments')
 261:         .where('service_id', isEqualTo: id)
 262:         .where('status', whereIn: ['pending', 'confirmed'])
 263:         .limit(1)
 264:         .get();
 265:     if (activeSnap.docs.isNotEmpty) {
 266:       if (mounted) {
 267:         showDialog(
 268:           context: context,
 269:           builder: (_) => AlertDialog(
 270:             title: const Text('Exclusão bloqueada'),
 271:             content: Text(
 272:               'O serviço "$name" possui agendamentos ativos.\n\n'
 273:               'Cancele ou conclua todos os agendamentos antes de excluir.',
 274:             ),
 275:             actions: [
 276:               FilledButton(
 277:                 onPressed: () => Navigator.pop(context),
 278:                 child: const Text('Entendi'),
 279:               ),
 280:             ],
 281:           ),
 282:         );
 283:       }
 284:       return;
 285:     }
 286:     if (!mounted) return;
 287:     final confirm = await showDialog<bool>(
 288:       context: context,
 289:       builder: (_) => AlertDialog(
 290:         title: const Text('Excluir serviço'),
 291:         content: Text('Deseja excluir "$name"?'),
 292:         actions: [
 293:           TextButton(
 294:             onPressed: () => Navigator.pop(context, false),
 295:             child: const Text('Cancelar'),
 296:           ),
 297:           FilledButton(
 298:             style: FilledButton.styleFrom(backgroundColor: Colors.red),
 299:             onPressed: () => Navigator.pop(context, true),
 300:             child: const Text('Excluir'),
 301:           ),
 302:         ],
 303:       ),
 304:     );
 305:     if (confirm == true) {
 306:       await _db.collection('services').doc(id).delete();
 307:     }
 308:   }
 309:   // ── Build ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
 310:   @override
 311:   Widget build(BuildContext context) {
 312:     return Scaffold(
 313:       appBar: AppBar(title: const Text('Serviços')),
 314:       floatingActionButton: FloatingActionButton(
 315:         onPressed: () => _showDialog(),
 316:         child: const Icon(Icons.add),
 317:       ),
 318:       body: StreamBuilder<QuerySnapshot>(
 319:         stream: _db
 320:             .collection('services')
 321:             .orderBy('sort_order')
 322:             .snapshots(),
 323:         builder: (_, snap) {
 324:           if (snap.connectionState == ConnectionState.waiting) {
 325:             return const Center(child: CircularProgressIndicator());
 326:           }
 327:           final docs = snap.data?.docs ?? [];
 328:           return ListView.builder(
 329:             itemCount: docs.length,
 330:             itemBuilder: (_, i) {
 331:               final doc = docs[i];
 332:               final d = doc.data() as Map<String, dynamic>;
 333:               final name = d['name'] as String? ?? '';
 334:               final price = d['price'] as num? ?? 0;
 335:               final duration = d['duration_minutes'] as num? ?? 0;
 336:               final isActive = d['is_active'] as bool? ?? true;
 337:               final iconUrl = d['icon_url'] as String? ?? '';
 338:               final sortOrder = d['sort_order'] as int? ?? 0;
 339:               return ListTile(
 340:                 leading: _ListIcon(iconUrl: iconUrl, isActive: isActive),
 341:                 title: Text(name),
 342:                 subtitle: Text(
 343:                   '#$sortOrder — ${formatBrl(price.toDouble())} — ${duration}min',
 344:                 ),
 345:                 trailing: Row(
 346:                   mainAxisSize: MainAxisSize.min,
 347:                   children: [
 348:                     Switch(
 349:                       value: isActive,
 350:                       onChanged: (_) => _toggleActive(doc.id, isActive),
 351:                     ),
 352:                     IconButton(
 353:                       icon: const Icon(Icons.edit_outlined),
 354:                       onPressed: () => _showDialog(id: doc.id, data: d),
 355:                     ),
 356:                     IconButton(
 357:                       icon: const Icon(Icons.delete_outline,
 358:                           color: Colors.red),
 359:                       onPressed: () => _delete(doc.id, name),
 360:                     ),
 361:                   ],
 362:                 ),
 363:               );
 364:             },
 365:           );
 366:         },
 367:       ),
 368:     );
 369:   }
 370: }
 371: // ── Widgets auxiliares ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
 372: class _IconPreview extends StatelessWidget {
 373:   final String networkUrl;
 374:   final XFile? localFile;
 375:   const _IconPreview({required this.networkUrl, this.localFile});
 376:   @override
 377:   Widget build(BuildContext context) {
 378:     Widget image;
 379:     if (localFile != null) {
 380:       image = Image.file(
 381:         File(localFile!.path),
 382:         width: 64,
 383:         height: 64,
 384:         fit: BoxFit.contain,
 385:       );
 386:     } else if (networkUrl.isNotEmpty) {
 387:       image = Image.network(
 388:         networkUrl,
 389:         width: 64,
 390:         height: 64,
 391:         fit: BoxFit.contain,
 392:         errorBuilder: (_, _, _) =>
 393:             const Icon(Icons.broken_image_outlined, size: 48),
 394:       );
 395:     } else {
 396:       image = const Icon(Icons.image_outlined, size: 48, color: Colors.grey);
 397:     }
 398:     return Center(
 399:       child: Container(
 400:         width: 80,
 401:         height: 80,
 402:         decoration: BoxDecoration(
 403:           border: Border.all(color: Colors.grey.shade300),
 404:           borderRadius: BorderRadius.circular(12),
 405:         ),
 406:         child: ClipRRect(
 407:           borderRadius: BorderRadius.circular(11),
 408:           child: image,
 409:         ),
 410:       ),
 411:     );
 412:   }
 413: }
 414: class _ListIcon extends StatelessWidget {
 415:   final String iconUrl;
 416:   final bool isActive;
 417:   const _ListIcon({required this.iconUrl, required this.isActive});
 418:   @override
 419:   Widget build(BuildContext context) {
 420:     if (iconUrl.isNotEmpty) {
 421:       return Image.network(
 422:         iconUrl,
 423:         width: 32,
 424:         height: 32,
 425:         fit: BoxFit.contain,
 426:         errorBuilder: (_, _, _) =>
 427:             const Icon(Icons.car_repair, size: 32),
 428:       );
 429:     }
 430:     return Icon(
 431:       isActive ? Icons.local_car_wash : Icons.local_car_wash_outlined,
 432:       color: isActive ? Colors.green : Colors.grey,
 433:     );
 434:   }
 435: }
 436: // ── Helpers BRL ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
 437: double _parseBrl(String text) {
 438:   final clean = text.replaceAll('.', '').replaceAll(',', '.');
 439:   return double.tryParse(clean) ?? 0.0;
 440: }
 441: class _BrlCurrencyFormatter extends TextInputFormatter {
 442:   final _fmt = NumberFormat('#,##0.00', 'pt_BR');
 443:   @override
 444:   TextEditingValue formatEditUpdate(
 445:       TextEditingValue oldValue, TextEditingValue newValue) {
 446:     final digits = newValue.text.replaceAll(RegExp(r'[^0-9]'), '');
 447:     if (digits.isEmpty) return newValue.copyWith(text: '');
 448:     final cents = int.tryParse(digits) ?? 0;
 449:     final formatted = _fmt.format(cents / 100);
 450:     return newValue.copyWith(
 451:       text: formatted,
 452:       selection: TextSelection.collapsed(offset: formatted.length),
 453:     );
 454:   }
 455: }

 193:   Future<void> _saveEdits() async {

 195:     if (name.isEmpty) {
 196:       ScaffoldMessenger.of(context).showSnackBar(

 199:       return;
 200:     }

 215:           SnackBar(content: Text('Erro ao salvar: $e')),
 216:         );
 217:       }
 218:     } finally {
 219:       if (mounted) setState(() => _saving = false);
 220:     }
 221:   }
 222:   Future<void> _toggleRole() async {
 223:     final newRole =

 247:   }
 248:   Future<void> _delete() async {
 249:     int activeCount = 0;
 250:     try {
 251:       final all = await widget.appointmentRepo
 252:           .getAppointmentsByCustomer(widget.user.uid);
 253:       activeCount = all
 254:           .where((a) =>
 255:               a.status == 'pending' || a.status == 'confirmed')
 256:           .length;
 257:     } catch (_) {}
 258:     if (!mounted) return;
 259:     final confirm = await showDialog<bool>(
 260:       context: context,
 261:       builder: (_) => AlertDialog(
 262:         title: const Text('Excluir usuario'),

 279:                 children: [
 280:                   const Text(
 281:                     'Isso vai causar:',
 282:                     style: TextStyle(fontWeight: FontWeight.bold),
 283:                   ),
 284:                   const SizedBox(height: 6),
 285:                   if (activeCount > 0)
 286:                     Text(
 287:                       '• $activeCount agendamento(s) ativo(s) serao cancelados e os slots liberados',
 288:                     ),
 289:                   const Text(
 290:                       '• Todos os agendamentos do usuario serao excluidos'),
 291:                   const Text(
 292:                       '• O documento do usuario sera removido'),
 293:                   const SizedBox(height: 6),
 294:                   const Text(
 295:                     'Esta acao nao pode ser desfeita.',
 296:                     style: TextStyle(fontWeight: FontWeight.bold),
 297:                   ),
 298:                 ],
 299:               ),
 300:             ),
 301:           ],
 302:         ),
 303:         actions: [
 304:           TextButton(
 305:               onPressed: () => Navigator.pop(context, false),
 306:               child: const Text('Cancelar')),
 307:           FilledButton(
 308:             style:
 309:                 FilledButton.styleFrom(backgroundColor: AppColors.error),
 310:             onPressed: () => Navigator.pop(context, true),
 311:             child: const Text('Excluir'),
 312:           ),
 313:         ],
 314:       ),
 315:     );
 316:     if (confirm == true) {
 317:       setState(() => _saving = true);
 318:       try {
 319:         await widget.appointmentRepo
 320:             .cancelAndDeleteAllByCustomer(widget.user.uid);
 321:         await widget.userRepo.deleteUserData(widget.user.uid);
 322:         widget.onChanged();
 323:         if (mounted) {
 324:           Navigator.pop(context);
 325:           ScaffoldMessenger.of(context).showSnackBar(
 326:             const SnackBar(content: Text('Usuario excluido.')),
 327:           );
 328:         }
 329:       } catch (e) {
 330:         if (mounted) {
 331:           ScaffoldMessenger.of(context).showSnackBar(
 332:             SnackBar(content: Text('Erro ao excluir: $e')),

 334:         }

 336:         if (mounted) setState(() => _saving = false);
 337:       }
 338:     }
 339:   }

 360:             // Informações somente leitura

 375:                     _label('Email (somente leitura)'),

 462:                 fontWeight: FontWeight.bold)),
 463:       );

 465: // ─────────────────────────────────────────
 466: // Tela de criação de novo usuário
 467: // ─────────────────────────────────────────
 468: class _CreateUserScreen extends StatefulWidget {
 469:   final UserRepository userRepo;
 470:   final VoidCallback onCreated;
 471:   const _CreateUserScreen({
 472:     required this.userRepo,
 473:     required this.onCreated,
 474:   });
 475:   @override
 476:   State<_CreateUserScreen> createState() => _CreateUserScreenState();
 477: }
 478: class _CreateUserScreenState extends State<_CreateUserScreen> {
 479:   final _nameCtrl = TextEditingController();
 480:   final _emailCtrl = TextEditingController();
 481:   final _passwordCtrl = TextEditingController();
 482:   String _role = 'customer';
 483:   bool _loading = false;
 484:   bool _obscure = true;
 485:   @override
 486:   void dispose() {
 487:     _nameCtrl.dispose();
 488:     _emailCtrl.dispose();
 489:     _passwordCtrl.dispose();
 490:     super.dispose();
 491:   }
 492:   Future<void> _create() async {
 493:     final name = _nameCtrl.text.trim();
 494:     final email = _emailCtrl.text.trim();
 495:     final password = _passwordCtrl.text;
 496:     if (name.isEmpty || email.isEmpty || password.length < 6) {
 497:       ScaffoldMessenger.of(context).showSnackBar(
 498:         const SnackBar(
 499:             content: Text(
 500:                 'Preencha nome, email e senha (minimo 6 caracteres).')),
 501:       );
 502:       return;
 503:     }
 504:     setState(() => _loading = true);
 505:     // Usa app secundário para não deslogar o admin
 506:     FirebaseApp? secondaryApp;
 507:     try {
 508:       secondaryApp = await Firebase.initializeApp(
 509:         name: 'AdminCreatedUser_${DateTime.now().millisecondsSinceEpoch}',
 510:         options: DefaultFirebaseOptions.currentPlatform,
 511:       );
 512:       final secondaryAuth =
 513:           FirebaseAuth.instanceFor(app: secondaryApp);
 514:       final cred = await secondaryAuth.createUserWithEmailAndPassword(
 515:         email: email,
 516:         password: password,
 517:       );
 518:       final uid = cred.user!.uid;
 519:       await widget.userRepo.createUser(UserModel(
 520:         uid: uid,
 521:         name: name,
 522:         email: email,
 523:         role: _role,
 524:         identifier: email.toLowerCase(),
 525:         identifierType: 'email',
 526:       ));
 527:       // Bug 5: grava entrada em identifiers para que o login funcione
 528:       await FirebaseService().firestore
 529:           .collection('identifiers')
 530:           .doc(email.toLowerCase())
 531:           .set({
 532:         'uid': uid,
 533:         'identifier_type': 'email',
 534:       });
 535:       widget.onCreated();
 536:       if (mounted) {
 537:         Navigator.pop(context);
 538:         ScaffoldMessenger.of(context).showSnackBar(
 539:           SnackBar(content: Text('Usuario "$name" criado com sucesso.')),
 540:         );
 541:       }
 542:     } catch (e) {
 543:       if (mounted) {
 544:         ScaffoldMessenger.of(context).showSnackBar(
 545:           SnackBar(content: Text('Erro ao criar usuario: $e')),
 546:         );
 547:       }
 548:     } finally {
 549:       await secondaryApp?.delete();
 550:       if (mounted) setState(() => _loading = false);
 551:     }
 552:   }
 553:   @override
 554:   Widget build(BuildContext context) {
 555:     return Scaffold(
 556:       appBar: AppBar(title: const Text('Novo Usuario')),
 557:       body: SingleChildScrollView(
 558:         padding: const EdgeInsets.all(
 559:             AppDimensions.screenPaddingHorizontal),
 560:         child: Column(
 561:           crossAxisAlignment: CrossAxisAlignment.stretch,
 562:           children: [
 563:             const SizedBox(height: AppDimensions.paddingLarge),
 564:             TextFormField(
 565:               controller: _nameCtrl,
 566:               decoration: const InputDecoration(
 567:                 labelText: 'Nome completo',
 568:                 border: OutlineInputBorder(),
 569:                 prefixIcon: Icon(Icons.person_outline),
 570:               ),
 571:               textCapitalization: TextCapitalization.words,
 572:             ),
 573:             const SizedBox(height: AppDimensions.paddingSmall),
 574:             TextFormField(
 575:               controller: _emailCtrl,
 576:               decoration: const InputDecoration(
 577:                 labelText: 'Email',
 578:                 border: OutlineInputBorder(),
 579:                 prefixIcon: Icon(Icons.email_outlined),
 580:               ),
 581:               keyboardType: TextInputType.emailAddress,
 582:             ),
 583:             const SizedBox(height: AppDimensions.paddingSmall),
 584:             TextFormField(
 585:               controller: _passwordCtrl,
 586:               obscureText: _obscure,
 587:               decoration: InputDecoration(
 588:                 labelText: 'Senha',
 589:                 border: const OutlineInputBorder(),
 590:                 prefixIcon: const Icon(Icons.lock_outline),
 591:                 suffixIcon: IconButton(
 592:                   icon: Icon(
 593:                       _obscure ? Icons.visibility_off : Icons.visibility),
 594:                   onPressed: () =>
 595:                       setState(() => _obscure = !_obscure),
 596:                 ),
 597:               ),
 598:             ),
 599:             const SizedBox(height: AppDimensions.paddingMedium),
 600:             DropdownButtonFormField<String>(
 601:               initialValue: _role,
 602:               decoration: const InputDecoration(
 603:                 labelText: 'Perfil',
 604:                 border: OutlineInputBorder(),
 605:                 prefixIcon: Icon(Icons.manage_accounts_outlined),
 606:               ),
 607:               items: const [
 608:                 DropdownMenuItem(
 609:                     value: 'customer', child: Text('Usuario')),
 610:                 DropdownMenuItem(
 611:                     value: 'master', child: Text('Master')),
 612:               ],
 613:               onChanged: (v) {
 614:                 if (v != null) setState(() => _role = v);
 615:               },
 616:             ),
 617:             const SizedBox(height: AppDimensions.paddingLarge),
 618:             ElevatedButton(
 619:               onPressed: _loading ? null : _create,
 620:               child: _loading
 621:                   ? const SizedBox(
 622:                       height: 20,
 623:                       width: 20,
 624:                       child: CircularProgressIndicator(strokeWidth: 2),
 625:                     )
 626:                   : const Text('Criar usuario'),
 627:             ),
 628:           ],
 629:         ),
 630:       ),
 631:     );
 632:   }
 633: }

ARQUIVO: C:\Users\Alex Salles\Apps - desenvolvimento\lavamax\lib\presentation\widgets\sprite_icon.dart
==================================================
   1: import 'dart:ui' as ui;
   2: import 'package:flutter/material.dart';
   3: import 'package:flutter/services.dart';
   4: /// Coordenadas de cada ícone dentro do sprite sheet services_sprite.png.
   5: /// Gerado automaticamente — não editar manualmente.
   6: const double _kIconSize = 96.0;
   7: const Map<String, Offset> _kSpriteMap = {
   8:   'customizacao':       Offset(0,   0),
   9:   'funilaria':          Offset(96,  0),
  10:   'higienizacao':       Offset(192, 0),
  11:   'home_car_detail':    Offset(288, 0),
  12:   'lavagem_premium':    Offset(0,   96),
  13:   'limpeza_motor':      Offset(96,  96),
  14:   'martelinho':         Offset(192, 96),
  15:   'peliculas':          Offset(288, 96),
  16:   'polimentos':         Offset(0,   192),
  17:   'ppf':                Offset(96,  192),
  18:   'restauracao_farois': Offset(192, 192),
  19:   'rodas':              Offset(288, 192),
  20:   'vitrificacao':       Offset(0,   288),
  21: };
  22: // Cache global da imagem — carregada uma única vez em toda a sessão.
  23: ui.Image? _cachedSprite;
  24: bool _loading = false;
  25: final List<VoidCallback> _listeners = [];
  26: Future<void> _loadSprite() async {
  27:   if (_cachedSprite != null || _loading) return;
  28:   _loading = true;
  29:   final data = await rootBundle.load('assets/images/services_sprite.png');
  30:   final codec = await ui.instantiateImageCodec(data.buffer.asUint8List());
  31:   final frame = await codec.getNextFrame();
  32:   _cachedSprite = frame.image;
  33:   _loading = false;
  34:   for (final cb in _listeners) {
  35:     cb();
  36:   }
  37:   _listeners.clear();
  38: }
  39: /// Exibe um ícone recortado do sprite sheet local services_sprite.png.
  40: /// [iconKey] é o nome do arquivo sem extensão (ex: 'polimentos').
  41: /// [size] é o tamanho de exibição em pixels lógicos.
  42: class SpriteIcon extends StatefulWidget {
  43:   final String iconKey;
  44:   final double size;
  45:   const SpriteIcon({
  46:     super.key,
  47:     required this.iconKey,
  48:     this.size = 40,
  49:   });
  50:   @override
  51:   State<SpriteIcon> createState() => _SpriteIconState();
  52: }
  53: class _SpriteIconState extends State<SpriteIcon> {
  54:   @override
  55:   void initState() {
  56:     super.initState();
  57:     if (_cachedSprite == null) {
  58:       _listeners.add(() {
  59:         if (mounted) setState(() {});
  60:       });
  61:       _loadSprite();
  62:     }
  63:   }
  64:   @override
  65:   Widget build(BuildContext context) {
  66:     final offset = _kSpriteMap[widget.iconKey];
  67:     final sprite = _cachedSprite;
  68:     if (sprite == null || offset == null) {
  69:       return SizedBox(
  70:         width: widget.size,
  71:         height: widget.size,
  72:         child: const Center(child: CircularProgressIndicator(strokeWidth: 2)),
  73:       );
  74:     }
  75:     return CustomPaint(
  76:       size: Size(widget.size, widget.size),
  77:       painter: _SpritePainter(
  78:         sprite: sprite,
  79:         srcOffset: offset,
  80:         iconSize: _kIconSize,
  81:         destSize: widget.size,
  82:       ),
  83:     );
  84:   }
  85: }
  86: class _SpritePainter extends CustomPainter {
  87:   final ui.Image sprite;
  88:   final Offset srcOffset;
  89:   final double iconSize;
  90:   final double destSize;
  91:   const _SpritePainter({
  92:     required this.sprite,
  93:     required this.srcOffset,
  94:     required this.iconSize,
  95:     required this.destSize,
  96:   });
  97:   @override
  98:   void paint(Canvas canvas, Size size) {
  99:     final src = Rect.fromLTWH(srcOffset.dx, srcOffset.dy, iconSize, iconSize);
 100:     final dst = Rect.fromLTWH(0, 0, destSize, destSize);
 101:     canvas.drawImageRect(sprite, src, dst, Paint());
 102:   }
 103:   @override
 104:   bool shouldRepaint(_SpritePainter old) =>
 105:       old.sprite != sprite || old.srcOffset != srcOffset || old.destSize != destSize;
 106: }
